Important News

French Legal Persons Attempt to Occupy Laoxikai in Tianjin

Tianjin Correspondence: The Laoxikai area within the Second District and Sixth Precinct of Tianjin originally belonged to our country's jurisdiction. It was previously occupied by French legal persons, causing negotiations. After the Tianjin Incident occurred last year, the French Concession authorities initially set up outposts in the area in the name of protecting local security. Then, they effectively occupied the area, recruiting 120 Chinese police officers and establishing the Second Branch of the French Police in Tianjin. Starting from the first day of last month, they ordered all local residents and shops to pay taxes. After receiving the report, the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately sent Inspector Wang Song to investigate. According to the report, in the fifth year of the Republic of China, France intended to expand the concession by using Laoxikai as a base. This was opposed by the entire Chinese people and the entire strike by Chinese workers in the French Concession, and it remains an unresolved issue to this day. After investigating Laoxikai, which originally belonged to the Second District and Sixth Precinct, it has requested the former Director Ceng to negotiate with the French Consul. However, there was no result. During the Tianjin Incident this year, France took this opportunity and occupied Laoxikai in December. All houses and shops were required to pay taxes, and 120 Chinese police officers were recruited. Twenty-seven outposts were set up in the area, and the Second Branch of the French Police in Tianjin was established at 59 Yongji Li, etc. Then, Liu Zhicun, the leader of the Investigation Division, was sent to investigate again. According to the report, according to the Gengzi Treaty, the border of the French Concession was limited by the Qiangzi River. At that time, there were many desolate areas within the Qiangzi River, and the French had no intention of aggression. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, the French Consul Bao set up outposts in the so-called Laoxikai area outside the Qiangzi River using force. At that time, our Chinese police also set up a branch outside the Qiangzi River. Consul Bao used force to abduct our police to the French Bureau of Public Works. The people of Tianjin were furious for a while and established the National Land Maintenance Association to implement a strike against France and established a strike group. All Chinese who used French legal persons in the French Concession went on strike. The French Consul was extremely tough and deployed troops to defend, as if facing a formidable enemy. Later, the French Minister and the French government feared that a war would be provoked by a small matter and telegraphed the French Consul to privately release the captured Chinese police, and the guns were confiscated. The weapons are still in the French Bureau of Public Works to this day. This is one point of national humiliation. Afterwards, two, three, or four months later, the workers' strike group lacked funds and gradually disbanded. Consul Bao transferred from Tianjin, and Consul Gan, along with Yang Yide, the Chinese police chief at the time, peacefully resolved the issue. The workers also gradually resumed work. As a result, the French Bureau of Public Works gradually set up outposts outside the Qiangzi River, and the French never set up outposts further west. And our police, from that time on, invisibly cancelled the establishment of police outposts and secretly abandoned Laoxikai. For several years, the land and houses outside the Qiangzi River have no Chinese contracts, nor do they have French contracts to the French Church, only receipts are used as proof, but ninety percent of the Laoxikai area is controlled by the French Church. Regarding police power, the French Concession method has implicitly become the area in front of and behind the church. In the past, although Laoxikai did not set up outposts, it has repeatedly handled cases and investigated household registration on behalf of the area, and the area has gradually become prosperous. However, there is no house or shop tax, which is equivalent to a no-man's-land. In recent years, only the Chinese provincial government has required five jiao of foreign currency per mu and per person in the area. As for people's lawsuits, they still go to the French Bureau of Public Works, and France also accepts them. When our country's courts summon cases, they must be registered at the French Bureau of Public Works. At that time, both sides were in a hesitant state. Since the Tianjin Incident this time, the French Bureau of Public Works has fooled a number of local people and requested the establishment of outposts. The French Bureau of Public Works added outposts in this way and openly recognized the area as a concession. They began to collect industry and patrol taxes from December 1 of this year and set to collect taxes according to the regulations of the concession starting from January. Our people suspect that our government has given it away, and the people inside dare not ask about the street lights in the area. The electricity company has been selling electricity, but the French Concession has never dared to sell electricity. Now the French are discussing getting their hands on changing the Laoxikai map and incorporating it into the concession, which is completely contrary to the treaty, etc. After investigating and confirming the facts, the Municipal Public Security Bureau submitted a request to the Municipal Government at the end of last year to negotiate with the French. On the 9th of this month, the Municipal Government sent a letter to the French Consul General to raise questions. Yesterday (13th) at 11:00 am, the French Consul replied to the Municipal Government, stating that the French Bureau of Public Works was maintaining public order in Laoxikai and denied that they had collected taxes. At 3:00 pm, the French Bureau of Public Works sent Detective Chief Rao to meet with Liu Butong of the Municipal Party Headquarters to explain that the French set up outposts in Laoxikai because people requested them during the chaos. They acted out of good intentions to maintain local order, so the French Bureau of Public Works did not interfere with the people's actions. It was all handled by the Public Assembly, that is, the French Bureau of Public Works did not collect taxes, etc. The Municipal Government's letter and the French Consul's reply are recorded as follows:

▲Municipal Government's Letter to the French Consul: Dear Sir, According to the Public Security Bureau's report, the Laoxikai area under the jurisdiction of the Second District and Sixth Precinct, during the Tianjin Incident on November 8 last year, the French Patrol Police took this opportunity to recruit 120 Chinese police officers and set up more than 20 outposts in the area. The Second Branch of the French Police in Tianjin was established at 59 Yongji Li, and various house and shop taxes were collected starting from December 1. This matter concerns national sovereignty, and we are obliged to submit a report for your review. The Tianjin Special Municipal Party Committee also sent a letter with the same reason. The Laoxikai area is under our country's jurisdiction, and the boundaries are clear. The treaty is there, and it cannot be confused. According to reports, during the Tianjin Incident, your side even had the incident of overstepping boundaries, expanding police power, and collecting taxes. Based on the previous information, in addition to issuing separate instructions and replying in writing, we should send a letter to your honorable Consul for review, asking whether the establishment of bureaus, outposts, and tax collection by your side in Laoxikai are true and what the situation is. To maintain friendship, this is addressed to Li Bili, the French Consul General in Tianjin.

▲French Consul's Reply: Dear Sir, I have received your government's letter of January 9, which stated, etc., in detail. The fact that the French Police Bureau maintains public order in the Laoxikai area is not a new fact. This issue has been decided for years and has been agreed upon with the Chinese authorities. There is no change to this. During the recent disturbances, at the request of the people and in response to the gradual increase in requests from the Chinese Police Bureau and the Chinese Court, the number of police officers has only increased. Furthermore, your officials have expressed their gratitude to our side. As for the issue of donations, I am very confused by the accusations. The French Bureau of Public Works has not collected any taxes in Laoxikai, nor will it collect them in the future. The details of its management are in the hands of the Public Council. This is just a malicious attack, which I, the Consul, have already requested your Mayor to pay attention to in my letter of January 6, 1932. I believe your Mayor will be able to take strict measures to stop it. This is addressed to Mayor Zhou of Tianjin, French Consul General in Tianjin, Li Bili, January 13, 1932.

Hubei Provincial Committee Cancels Resignation Intentions

▲However, the Finance Director's Determination to Leave Remains Strong

Hankou Correspondence: Since Chiang Kai-shek resigned and returned home, and the unified government was completed, the issue of the reorganization of the Hubei Provincial Government has become the focus of public attention. At the same time, the saying of the Nine-Province Joint Defense was widely spread in Beijing and Shanghai, making outsiders want to know the truth. The Yangtze and Han Rivers can originally be used to tip the scale. When He Yingqin and He Chengjun denied this matter, the doubts of the public gradually dissipated, but there was still no strong proof of the reorganization of the Hubei Provincial Government. Recently, it was suddenly reported that He Chengjun and the entire Provincial Committee had submitted a general resignation to the central government. After many inquiries, it was learned that He and the entire Provincial Committee did have this proposal at first, and the presentation had already been drafted. However, due to the urgency of diplomacy and the importance of provincial administration, they cancelled their intentions to resign. The central government also relied heavily on them. Sun Ke, the President of the Executive Yuan, sent Representative Zhang Guoyuan to Hankou on the 10th to discuss with He, which was quite satisfactory. He returned to Beijing yesterday to report. Currently, He and the directors of the Civil Affairs, Construction, and Education Departments go to the Provincial Government and various departments every day to handle affairs and are very enthusiastic. However, Wu Guozhen, the Director of Finance, is very determined to resign. On the 13th, Wu submitted his resignation to the Provincial Government again, stating that "Guozhen has shallow knowledge and mediocre talent, and has mistakenly managed the treasury. I should try my best to serve with diligence to repay your appreciation. However, since the beginning of my appointment, I have been faced with accumulated deficits. I have tried every means to maintain the status quo. I hoped that I would have some time to reorganize so that all tax revenues would increase and all expenditures would be less difficult. However, since the summer, there have been continuous rains and disasters, and in the autumn, the embankments have collapsed. The tax sources have been cut off, and disaster relief is not possible. Recently, the Northeast has fallen, the national crisis is in full swing, and the financial situation is extremely tight, which is rare in history. The central government subsidies and special tax agreements that I relied on in the past have been difficult to pay on time. The loans that I relied on to seek relief have been exhausted, and the mortgages have been used up. For months, I have been worried that I would not be able to support the security, and I have been worrying about it day and night, and my mind and body are exhausted. Although the New Year has been barely passed, the great difficulties of the coming days cannot be dealt with by my strength. I am afraid that there will be some delays, and the impact will be significant. I should resign and retreat to make way for the capable. I should submit a request for your review and forwarding to the higher authorities, and send someone to take over in advance." The Provincial Government discussed this at the political affairs meeting on the 14th and resolved to retain him. Due to the lack of government funds, it was decided to borrow rent for one month in Wuchang, Hanyang, and Hankou, using the unpaid subsidies from the central government for October, November, and December of last year as a principal repayment fund. If the subsidies cannot be received within three months, the 3 million short-term rehabilitation bonds previously approved by the central government will be used to repay. At the same time, the loan rent will be used as collateral to borrow 800,000 yuan from the Hankou General Chamber of Commerce to meet emergency needs. At the same time, it was also decided to increase the tax rate on business tax. The original rate of 10 per mille will be collected as before, and the 5 per mille will be increased to 6 per mille. The 2.5 per mille and below will be doubled, and the Finance Department will submit it to the Provincial Government for approval and implementation. (January 15)

Guangdong Central Banknotes Experience a Run

▲ Authorities Actively Curb Panic to Calm the Situation

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the cessation of military operations in Guangdong Province, financial authorities have successively sought ways to maintain the value of banknotes issued in the province. The one-yuan denomination of the central banknotes has now resumed redemption, and the five-yuan denomination also resumed redemption on the 8th. If the situation stabilizes somewhat, the implementation would proceed smoothly. Unexpectedly, the day after the five-yuan banknotes resumed redemption, many rumors circulated in the market. Some rumors claimed that Wang Jingwei had resigned, and the situation might change drastically. Others claimed that the banknotes previously sealed up in the province would be unsealed on the 11th, and interest would be paid simultaneously. At that time, the market would be flooded with central banknotes, and the price of the central banknotes would inevitably be affected. Various opinions abounded, and no consensus could be reached. Therefore, those who usually held central banknotes rushed to the provincial bank (formerly the Guangdong Central Bank, which was reorganized into the Guangdong Provincial Bank on January 1st) to redeem them. From the morning of the 9th, the provincial bank was overwhelmed with redemption requests. By about 5 p.m., there were still two or three hundred people standing in front of the provincial bank. In order to maintain credit, the president of the provincial bank supervised the staff to expedite the process and redeem banknotes as quickly as they were received. It is reported that the provincial bank redeemed about 350,000 yuan in cash throughout the 9th. On the 10th, many exchange shops in the city dared not open for business, and they politely refused to redeem central banknotes by claiming they had no cash. Although shops dared not explicitly refuse to accept them, they secretly raised prices. As a result, the central banknotes that had been redeemed were discounted, and the price of those that had not been redeemed dropped from 97 to 91 cents on the dollar. However, observing the situation in Guangdong, the security is currently stable, and it is expected that this banknote panic will soon subside. On the day the panic suddenly erupted, the financial authorities immediately convened a meeting to discuss ways to curb the panic. In addition to Shen Zaihe and Huang Guanzhang, the president and vice president of the provincial bank, there were also representatives from the Department of Finance, such as Ye Qing and Liang Zhiguang. As a result, four measures were agreed upon: ㈠ The 10th is a bank holiday, and the provincial bank decided to comply by suspending redemption for one day. ㈡ Redemption will continue on the 11th. ㈢ All revenue collection agencies will strictly enforce the rule that taxes must be accepted in full with redeemed central banknotes. ㈣ The unsealing of the central banknotes on the 11th will be temporarily suspended, and the date for unsealing will be rescheduled after the panic subsides. Furthermore, in order to fundamentally maintain the credit of the banknotes, the Department of Finance is implementing the third phase of its plan to maintain the value of the central banknotes. This plan involves issuing 5 million yuan in prize-bearing bonds, divided into 1 million bonds, each worth 5 yuan, with the province's consolidated tax revenue as collateral. A lottery will be drawn each month to repay the principal and pay interest, with 530,000 yuan of consolidated tax revenue allocated each time to be managed by a fund management committee as a fixed fund. The temporary solution is to use the 10 million yuan in funds currently held by the provincial bank for redemption, and to entrust reputable banks to redeem the banknotes on its behalf. It has been verified that the regulations for the issuance of 5 million yuan in prize-bearing bonds to maintain the value of the central banknotes were announced by the Department of Finance on the 9th, and the issuance will begin on the 15th. (January 11th)

Local Dispatches

Fengxian

The Origin of the Bandit Scare in Tuolin: The county Public Security Bureau has investigated and reported that the bandit scare in Tuolin is inaccurate. However, regarding the origin of the rumors, according to a report from Ma Teng, the director of the seventh branch of the local Public Security Bureau, a large gang of salt smugglers suddenly arrived in the area several days ago. There were two or three hundred of them, and they were buying smuggled salt in various coastal towns, loading it onto ships, and planning to export it. The salt police authorities discovered the situation and immediately dispatched an anti-smuggling patrol team to intervene. However, the smugglers firmly insisted that if the authorities did not accommodate them, they would rather fight to the death. The police team, in addition to mobilizing its forces to prepare for a thorough suppression, also notified the Public Security Bureaus of Songjiang and Fengxian counties, informing the public not to panic. Fortunately, local figures intervened to mediate, averting a disaster, but the community had already suffered a considerable scare. It is now learned that, in order to maintain security along the coast, the military and police authorities specially dispatched the first platoon of the first company of the fourth battalion of the Second Regiment of the Provincial Security Infantry from Jinshanwei to be stationed there yesterday to maintain order.

Songjiang

Rumors of Robbery of Weapons at Dajia Kiln: At about 5 p.m. on the 13th of this month, it was reported in Sijing that bandits had robbed weapons from the militia at Fangjia Kiln. All sectors of Sijing heightened precautions, and merchants and residents were very apprehensive. It was not until the next morning that it was learned that nothing of the sort had happened. However, the origin of this rumor and where it originated are currently under investigation.

Resolutions of the Party-Government Talks Conference: The county's Party-Government Talks Conference held a regular meeting today to discuss the following matters: ㈠ Hawkers along the streets in the Xicheng area of the city are obstructing traffic by setting up stalls for selling goods. Although the First District Office has consulted with the police district to take action, no results have been achieved. After discussion, it was decided to jointly advise the merchants to remove their stalls, and the police will take action. ㈡ Recently, robbery cases have occurred frequently in the urban and rural areas. How should preventive measures be carefully considered? It was resolved that the county government should send a letter to the military and police agencies to conduct a thorough investigation.

Suzhou

The Qian Family Robbery Suspects Brought to Suzhou: After Suzhou-Kunshan detectives arrested six suspects, Ye Fachun, Xu Changshu, Xue Daocai, Liu Bu, Jiang Yiwan, and Lu Weishu, in the Yangshupu area of Shanghai for the robbery of Qian Songyao's home in Sixiang Lane, they were handed over to the Kunshan Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (the 16th) at 3 p.m., they were escorted to Suzhou from Kunshan along with a Mauser pistol, 55 rounds of ammunition, and a briefcase. They were immediately handed over to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

The Dongwu Student Strike is Expected to Subside: Since Cheng Shugan and three other representatives from the Law School of Dongwu University in Shanghai came to Suzhou, they have been engaged in mediation. The conditions are that the school withdraws the expulsion order against Zhu Zong and that the students do not give a farewell party for President Yang. The two sides have a chance of coming to an agreement. Therefore, the situation yesterday (the 16th) had eased.

Jiangyin

Jimei Pawnshop Ceases Operations: Jimei Pawnshop in Jiangyin City was established in the ninth year of the Tongzhi reign of the late Qing Dynasty by Sheng and other shareholders from Changzhou. Since the Republic of China, pawnshops in Jiangyin City and the surrounding countryside have closed one after another. Jimei was the only one left in the city. Recently, Sheng's Yuzhai Charity Estate was completely dissolved. All properties owned and managed by the Charity Estate were resolved by the Charity Estate's board of directors to be liquidated separately. Jimei was also within the scope of the Yuzhai Charity Estate. After Manager Xu Xingxi received the notice, he scheduled the pawnshop to close on the 18th and handle the liquidation.

Nantong

The Truth Behind the Incineration of Opium Scandal is Difficult to Ascertain: Yan Changdang, a prosecutor from the Zhenjiang District Court, was ordered by the High Court to come to Nantong to thoroughly investigate the case of the county court incinerating opium and engaging in fraud. On the 15th, he opened a court session at the court to interrogate Zhang Rong and others involved in the case. There were 114 catties of opium belonging to Sun Deming, with 14.5 catties missing, and more than 2,000 taels of opium belonging to unnamed individuals, half of which were fake. The original list had 28 items, but suddenly 30 items were pointed out. There are many other points of suspicion, making it difficult to clarify the case for the time being.

The Provincial Committee Urges Payment of Transportation Bonds: The provincial authorities believe that Nantong has only paid 5,000 yuan for the purchased transportation bonds, with a significant difference in the amount due. A special committee has been sent to Nantong to urge payment.

The Director of the Construction Bureau is Accused of Negligence: Wu Wenhua, the director of the Nantong County Construction Bureau, has been accused by local residents of dereliction of duty and illegal acts. The province has ordered the county government to conduct a thorough investigation.

Wuxi

Long-Distance Bus Injures Female Worker: Xue Aqi, a rural woman from Jiejing, the fifth district of the county, was carrying twelve dozen pairs of yarn socks to the city to deliver to the Renyu Sock Factory at 9 a.m. yesterday when she was hit by the Wuxi-Chengjiang Long-Distance Bus Company's No. 9 bus near Yanqiao. The wheels rolled over her legs, and she immediately fainted. Her injuries were quite serious. The bus driver, Ping Hongliang, took her to the city and admitted her to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The Sock Industry Association learned of the incident and made serious representations to the Long-Distance Bus Company regarding the repeated accidents. The bus driver, Ping Hongliang, was handed over to the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau for temporary detention. A request was submitted to the county government, the Construction Bureau, and the Public Security Bureau for relief to protect human life.

Anti-Japanese Association Seizes Large Quantity of Japanese Coal: The Inspection Department of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association received a secret report the day before yesterday, stating that Yan Huozui, the manager of the Yitaixing Coal Company in Yefangchang, Beimen, was the most famous coal merchant in Wuxi, and had recently secretly imported a large quantity of Japanese coal, intending to sell it to various factories and ships. The two ministers, Li and Yang, immediately led all the inspectors to inspect the coal company and found more than 200 tons of Fushun Qihu Japanese coal. It was immediately sealed up, and the account books were taken to the association for review and punishment.

Changzhou

Fire at Fuda Yarn Factory: The Fuda Yarn Factory outside the East Gate of the county, due to the brisk sales of domestic yarn this year, has been operating day and night. Unexpectedly, a careless act occurred in the flower room at about 2 a.m. this morning (the 16th), and the fire spread rapidly. The fire brigade from each district rushed to extinguish the fire. It took about two hours to put out the fire. More than 40 flower rooms were burned down, and the losses were significant.

Rugao

Change of Director of the Bureau of Finance: Chen Rongshou, the newly appointed director of the county's Bureau of Finance, has not been in office for even half a month. Unexpectedly, the province has suddenly appointed Zhang Xianyi to take over, and Huang Runsheng has been appointed as the chief accountant. Zhang is scheduled to come to Rugao within a week to take office. Huang arrived in Rugao yesterday (the 11th).

Nineteen Villages of Dongzao Disaster Victims are Facing Starvation: This year's flood in the county was exceptionally severe, and the harvest was greatly reduced. Farmers in the Dongzao area of Juegang have had no harvest, and nineteen villages are facing starvation. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented in nearly a century. Currently, unscrupulous individuals are inciting the poor, organizing mahjong clubs, and actually "eating mahjong rice." It is not known how the authorities will provide relief.

More Than Eighty Fishermen are Buried at Sea: A fishing boat named Hengyuan, owned by Lu Wenzheng of Pengcha, had 85 fishermen on board. The other day, while the boat was sailing to the Changsha Port area to harvest sea snails, it was suddenly hit by a hurricane and capsized in the sea. All 85 people on board were killed, which is also a tragic event.

Notes on Robbery Cases: Wu Ertou, from Qianxiang Caojiaqiao in the Baipu District, makes a living by lending money. The other night, many bandits suddenly broke in, first hanging the victim on the railing, pouring kerosene on him, and setting him on fire to force him to reveal where the silver was hidden. As a result, a total of three gold and silver bracelets and more than 300 silver dollars were robbed. It is reported that the victim's lower body was severely burned. Also, the home of a Xu in Xiaoxujiazhuang, Jiang'an District, was suddenly attacked by many bandits on the night of the 9th. They carried various firearms and flashlights. After entering the house, they first hung Xu up and beat him, and stabbed his son with a knife. They then searched the house for clothes, silver, and other valuables. By the time the local militia heard the news and arrived, the bandits had already fled without a trace.

Zhenjiang

Compensation Dispute at Rentang Pawnshop in Jintan: Previously, the Rentang Pawnshop in Jintan County was robbed, and a fire was set. The county's party and government organs decided to compensate 80% of the value and deduct 1% interest, and submitted the decision to the Civil Affairs Department and the Construction Department for approval. Later, due to an appeal from the pawnshop's shareholders, the Civil Affairs Department and the Industry Department sent a telegram to the county on a good day, changing the compensation to 50%. This caused conflict between the pawnshop staff and the pawn customers. Police and civilians were injured. Currently, pawn customers have gathered, firmly requesting that the original plan of compensating 80% be followed. The situation is serious. If the telegram is not withdrawn, the dispute will escalate further. A special telegram has been sent to the provincial government and the Civil Affairs Department and the Industry Department, requesting that the original plan be followed and the county be ordered to comply.

Silver and Money Industry Maintains Financial Measures: The Provincial Department of Industry believes that the financial situation in the provincial capital is critical, and the market is unstable. On the evening of the 14th, it sent a telegram to the Zhenjiang County Government and the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, instructing them to jointly convene representatives of the silver and money industry to discuss solutions. At 4 p.m. on the 15th, the county government and the Chamber of Commerce complied and convened representatives for talks. More than 20 managers of banks and money shops attended. Lu Xiaobo, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, and Zhang Peng, the county magistrate, reported successively on the order to convene the meeting and the ban on the export of cash. Yan Junfu, a representative of the Bank of China, reported that the Bank of China had experienced a run due to people's mistaken belief in rumors, but the situation had calmed down. The representatives then expressed their determination to fully cooperate to maintain the financial stability of Zhenjiang. Regarding the year-end settlement at the end of January, the banks plan to request instructions from the head office. The six banks, including the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Jiangsu Bank, Shanghai Commercial Bank, and China Industrial Bank, will jointly provide 500,000 yuan in loans. The remaining funds will be raised by the money industry itself. It is reported that the money industry plans to borrow money from its counterparts in Shanghai and Suzhou to overcome the difficulties.

Qingjiang

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Wangying Town: Wangying Town, five miles north of the county seat of Huaiyin, has more than 3,000 merchant households. At 10 p.m. on the 11th, a group of bandits suddenly broke down the gate of Zhang Yutai Sauce Garden, owned by Zhang Shengzhi, in the western street of the town. They first seized the worker Wang Er, then entered the inner room, guarded Zhang Shengzhi's brother Zhang Wu, and kidnapped his five-year-old son and his aunt Wan. When the Zhang family went outside to call for help, the bandits had already fled to the northeast of Wangying.

Xiaoshan

Another Robbery Case in Hujianong, Southern Township: The home of Hu Guancai in Hujianong, about eight miles across the river from Linpu in the southern township of Xiaoshan County, was robbed by more than 20 bandits on the night of the 8th. They took away silver dollars, clothes, and other items worth about 1,000 yuan. On the same night, the home of Zhou Deqing in Hou Ni was also broken into by more than 10 bandits speaking with mixed accents and carrying muskets and knives. They took away more than 120 silver dollars, as well as gold rings, silver bracelets, silk fabrics, and leather coats, worth a total of more than 300 yuan. The victims have filed a report with the county government, requesting that the police teams on land and water cooperate in the investigation.

Letter from the Adjutant Office of the 121st Brigade

Sir, after reading your newspaper's Zhenjiang news column on the 15th of this month, which stated that the 121st Brigade reportedly sent a team to Wuchang wheel to seize more than 10,000 taels of opium, it was found that it was not entirely consistent with the facts. It is feared that the report from afar may be inaccurate. The details of that day are hereby sent to you in a letter, hoping that you will correct the record. On the 12th, according to a confidential report, bandits Qian Song and others secretly boarded the Wuchang wheel in Anqing, carrying dangerous goods, and came to Zhenjiang and Shanghai to form gangs, endangering security and order. In order to maintain security, this brigade could not but take precautions. Immediately, personnel were sent to the wheel together with customs officials from the Zhenjiang Customs to check. One person who looked suspicious was found and searched. Eight packages of opium were seized. This brigade, in addition to transferring the opium to the customs in accordance with the procedures to take back the receipt, and the Qiu comprador of the Wuchang wheel also signed a document proving the inspection of the eight packages of opium, the wheel did not have other losses, there was really no other situation. The so-called seizure of more than 10,000 taels of opium is even more untrue. The Adjutant Office of the 121st Brigade.

Record of the General Meeting of the Jiangsu Secondary School Joint Association

▲ Contributed 16 Points of Advice to Zhou Fo-hai

The general meeting of the Jiangsu Provincial Joint Association of Secondary Schools was held yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m. at the Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang High School. Nine, please have the provincial government firmly maintain the decision to recover 1.32 million in Zhongda funding, otherwise, the principals will have no choice but to resign collectively. Ten, limit the management office to move to the provincial capital within six months. Eleven, organize a committee to effectively rectify the public forests. Twelve, please have the provincial government clear the subsidy fee of 300,000 during the busy harvest season. Thirteen, please determine which disaster areas must be free. Fourteen, find a way to reissue the remainder of the temporary fee for the 18th year. Fifteen, plan the secondary education budget for the coming year as soon as possible. Sixteen, release the temporary fee for the 20th year. Before it is released, do not use it as regular expenses.

The Jiangsu Social Education Organization Joint Association Demands Money

Nanjing, 16th - The Jiangsu Provincial Social Education Organization Joint Association has sent separate telegrams to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and the Provincial Government's Department of Education regarding the Jiangsu Provincial education funding, proposing short-term and long-term solutions: ㈠ Please have the Ministry of Finance fulfill its commitment to make up for the 2.5 million yuan shortfall in land tax revenue in the four years before the 19th year, and allocate 1 million in cash or treasury bonds worth 1 million in cash before the end of this month to solve the immediate crisis. ㈡ Please have the Central Government allocate 150,000 yuan from the cigarette tax each month starting from January of this year to compensate for the Jiangsu education fee. ㈢ Please follow the budget regulations and the standards for dividing national and local revenues and expenditures promulgated by the National Government, and allocate the entire 1.32 million yuan of funding for the National Central University to be paid by the Ministry of Finance.

Anhui Province's Education Sector's Demand for Arrears is Increasingly Urgent

▲ Middle School Principals Go to the Executive Yuan and Ministry of Education to Petition

The presidents of Anhui Provincial Secondary Schools and the heads of social education institutions have come to Nanjing to demand arrears. Although the General Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance agreed to sign a report to Minister Huang, requesting that 100,000 yuan be issued, only 20,000 yuan was actually issued. The principals believe that only 20,000 yuan was issued out of a total of 445,000 yuan in arrears, which is less than 1/22 of the total amount, making it difficult to return to Anhui. Just as the Ministry of Finance was changing hands, it was decided to launch a large-scale movement after the new Minister of Finance takes office.

Nanjing, 16th - On the morning of the 16th, more than 20 principals, curators, and superintendents of various middle schools in Anhui Province went to the Ministry of Finance to demand arrears, but no one received them. They waited in the General Affairs Director's office until evening, left a note, and left. It is said that they intend to publish an open question to the Ministry of Finance, asking whether there is any way to solve the problem, and they also intend to unite with Tianjin, Beijing, Hubei, and other places to take action.

The Municipal Bureau of Education Holds Elementary School Teacher Registration

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued a notice regarding the registration of elementary school teachers for the fifth session, stating: "The regulations for the registration of elementary school teachers in this city were revised on June 10 of last year and submitted to the municipal government for approval and promulgation. Registration will be held from January 25 to January 27 of this year. The dates for the oral examination and physical examination are January 29 and 30. All current or prospective elementary school teachers in municipal and registered private elementary schools in this city who have not yet registered may register at the Bureau in accordance with the revised registration regulations. No supplementary registration will be made after the deadline. Please pay attention and do not make a mistake again. This notice is issued on January 16, 21st year of the Republic of China, by Director Xu Peihuang."

Ning Xin'er Falls to the Ground, Greatly Honors the Family, China Wins Against Malaya 6-1 in the First Battle

▲ Malaya Suffers in the First Half: China Scores Half a Dozen in a Row

▲ China Shows Respect in the Second Half: Malaya Recaptures a Goal

丨6,000 Fans Cheer丨Wishing China Success丨

The China team, which concentrated its heroes, was officially formed yesterday and competed against the Malayan Overseas Chinese Football Team at the China Baseball Field. Ning Xin'er fell to the ground, greatly honoring the family. It won 6-1. 6,000 fans could not help but cheer loudly, as if to wish China success in the future.

▲ China Team Lineup

Liang Shutang Qian Jingyong

Li Ning Tu Kaiyuan (Up) Chen Hongguang

Zhou Xianyan Feng Yunyou (Down) Dai Linjing

▲ Malayan Lineup

Liang Fulai Deng Yueyun

Why Distinguish Between Victory and Defeat in One Family

Yesterday's battle was originally between two sides of the same family. Victory and defeat are not worth counting. The focus is on China's individual talents and the teamwork of the entire team, as the basis for the lineup for future formal battles. The Malayan team is only a guest, but its defeat is due to the weakness of the center defense line, the instability of the inner defense, and the slowness of the forwards' actions. Only the goalkeeper's performance was amazing. He suffered a lot in the first half, losing six goals in a row. He struggled hard in the second half and won back one goal. It seems that China had a suspicion of respecting the guests. As a result, China won 6-1. Referee: Chen Jixiang

Two Goalkeepers, Different Levels of Ease

Zhou Xianyan of China and Huang Jinbai of Malaya are both goalkeepers with astonishing talent. However, due to the effectiveness of their respective internal defense and support, they experienced different levels of ease. Throughout the ninety minutes, Zhou Xianyan missed one save, which was his mistake. Ning Dao bravely cleared a dangerous shot, narrowly avoiding a disaster. The final goal conceded was simply Zhou showing hospitality as the home team. Huang Jinbai, on the other hand, became the target of public criticism, facing immense pressure and inevitably missing some shots. The fourth goal, when Chen Hongguang seized the opportunity to break through, was Huang's oversight. With the defense collapsing, one man alone could not hold it. The blame for the other five goals conceded lies with the ineffective support.

Old Partners Reunite After Long Separation

Li Ning and Feng Yunyou were old partners during the golden era of Yue Hua. Later, they pursued their own paths and went their separate ways. Now serving China, they reunite after a long separation, their interceptions and blocks forming an impenetrable defense. Jiang Shan's performance in the second half was also very satisfactory. In short, there was a world of difference. The five Malayan forwards constantly hit walls, truly feeling the despair of being unable to advance.

Central Defenders Excel in Both Offense and Defense

The most obvious difference between the two sides was the strength of their central defense lines. Malaya's Huang Kehou could handle one opponent, but he couldn't manage the overall situation due to his limited abilities. China's three players, however, were extremely effective. Tu Kaiyuan is undoubtedly the number one central defender among Chinese players today. Chen Jiaqiu and Liang Shutang excelled in both soft and hard defense, contributing to the six-goal lead in the first half. Changing the formation in the second half made them less cohesive than in the first half.

The Five Forwards Bursting with Energy

China's five forwards were all bursting with energy. Speaking objectively, Dai Linjing led the troops and followed every command. Feigning a shot, he broke the Malayan defense with his power. His specialty was delivering effective passes and providing timely support. Mei Hongbao, on the right wing, made significant contributions with his quick movements and well-timed crosses, a rare talent. Chen Hongguang's brilliance was evident as he scored three goals, accounting for half of the total. It seemed as if fortune was smiling upon him. Qian Jingyong has great potential, but his eagerness to win sometimes led to offside fouls. Chen Yutian was agile and scored a goal, leveraging his strengths. If Chen Zhenhe and Qiu Dongyan had been on the field, they would have undoubtedly put on some more amazing performances.

Six Goals in One Breath

Reviewing the course of the battle, in the first ten minutes, although China had the wind advantage, the situation was still stable. Then, Mei Hongbao crossed from the right to the left, Qian Hongguang stepped aside, Qian Jingyong passed it back, and Dai Linjing pushed it into the goal, breaking the deadlock. Subsequently, China scored one goal after another. Within three minutes, Chen Hongguang scored. Five minutes later, Dai's shot hit the goalpost and bounced in. Eight minutes later, Hongguang scored twice in a row. The final goal was kicked in by Chen Yutian, completing the half-dozen. Thus, the first half concluded.

Respectful Guest, a Consolation Goal

The Malayan forwards didn't initially exert their full effort, making it difficult to penetrate deep into the opposing territory and execute their shooting skills. In the second half, the Chinese forwards seemed intent on simply finishing the game, and the Malayan counterattacks increased. However, their slowness resulted in numerous missed opportunities in front of the goal. With accurate and powerful shots, they could have achieved more. At that time, Dai made three impressive shots, all effectively saved by the goalkeeper. In the end, Malaya's Guan Xinde scored a goal when the opponent showed no resistance, salvaging a narrow defeat. The result was a 6-1 loss for Malaya, their fourth defeat in Shanghai.

Yiyuan Deserted, Yue Hua Lost to Navy

▲ 2-4 | Group A Match

The Yue Hua football team lost to the British Navy by a score of 2-4 yesterday in the deserted Yiyuan. This Group A match saw an incomplete lineup and a lackluster performance, allowing the sailors to avenge their previous 7-1 defeat.

Desolate Scene

Excluding the players, there were fewer than thirty people in the vast stands. Newspaper reporters accounted for four of them, and the thirty also included the park's staff and attendants. There were no female spectators. The usual stream of cars was reduced to only three, creating a desolate atmosphere. Did people know Yue Hua would lose and fear disappointment?

Navy's Progress

The navy's team yesterday still consisted of players from the Kangwei and Liangwei ships. After losing to Yue Hua 1-7, they surprisingly defeated Lax 8-4 last Saturday, shocking many. Their skills had indeed improved significantly. They had many chances in front of Yue Hua's goal yesterday, but their poor shooting resulted in countless missed opportunities.

Yue Hua's Disarray

Yue Hua's lineup was disorganized yesterday, which was also a reason for their defeat. Many key players were absent, taking leave and going home. Several new players joined, which diminished their coordination and shooting, resulting in the sailors cornering them.

Course of Defeat

The first half ended 2-1, with the navy taking the lead. The second half also ended 2-1, making the final score 4-2, and Yue Hua lost. The navy's right inside forward, Hansen, scored first. Yue Hua's right winger, Chen Chao, tied the score. Stevens scored again, ending the first half. In the second half, Wan Xianghua received Yang Renwei's pass and tied the score again at 2-2. Unexpectedly, the navy scored two consecutive goals, with Hansen and Cox each scoring once, ending the game at 4-2.

Local News

Wu Tiecheng Continued Discussing Financial Problems with All Sectors Yesterday

▲ Even Closer Than Yesterday

Yesterday afternoon, representatives from all sectors continued the financial conference at Mayor Wu's residence. On the government side, Wu Tiecheng, Cai Zengji, Zhang Qun, and Chen Mingshu attended. On the representatives' side, besides Qin Runqing, who was unable to attend due to business and was replaced by Pei Yunqing, the remaining six were still Zhang Gongquan, Li Fukun, Wang Xiaolai, Shi Liangcai, Du Yuesheng, and Zhang Xiaolin. After adjourning the previous night, the representatives scrambled in all directions, raising five million. The meeting began at around 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The representatives reported on the fundraising situation. The government side still believed that it was far from sufficient and urged the representatives to work harder to raise more funds. At that time, the representatives put forward proposals, stating that the current situation was urgent. If they waited for the new Minister of Finance to take office, it would be too late. It would be better to ask Huang Hanliang and Lin Kanghou to temporarily not step down and handle the loan procedures. It was heard that the general idea of ​​their proposals was to consolidate the public debt fund on the one hand and ease the financial atmosphere on the other. From then on, the government's finances must be made public. In short, all the representatives were very willing to cooperate with the government in borrowing money and make efforts to proceed in the hope of maintaining the status quo of the government. Finally, Chen Mingshu stated that the proposal to suspend the payment of principal and interest on public debt was truly a last resort. If the finances could be managed, the government would definitely not want to resort to this tactic. The previous rumor that there were 20,000 soldiers who would use force if the loan could not be managed was a misunderstanding. Fortunately, through repeated meetings between the two sides, they were very close, so the government and the people would definitely be able to cooperate effectively in the future. It was said that a meeting would still be held today.

Wu Tiecheng's Talk

Mayor Wu Tiecheng issued a statement to reporters yesterday, saying that at 3 p.m. on the 15th, he made an appointment with the Shanghai financial community to discuss financial issues at the Bankers Association. A certain newspaper reported the situation at that time, and there were some discrepancies in his remarks. For example, he reported that "Sun Yat-sen and others returned to Beijing this time, originally intending to discuss the special committee, deciding to sever relations with Japan and stop paying principal and interest," and so on. He did not make these remarks. It must be understood that Sun Yat-sen took on the important responsibility of the executive this time and was responsible to the Central Political Council. With the national crisis at hand, the situation was becoming increasingly serious, and the three gentlemen, Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Jingwei, and Hu Hanmin, had not yet gone to Beijing. There was no way to adhere to the major policy. In order to cope with the current emergency situation, it was proposed to set up a special committee under the Central Political Council before the standing committee members of the Central Political Council arrived in Beijing. According to the policy decided by the Central Political Council, the emergency political affairs will be dealt with. As for the rumors from the outside that the government has implemented a policy of severing relations with Japan and stopping paying principal and interest, this is just an unavoidable method proposed by someone, and it is not a decided policy. People outside do not know the truth and think it is a fact. This is where the rumor comes from.

Wang Jingwei Leaves Hospital and Goes to Hangzhou to Meet Chiang Yesterday

▲ Ms. Chen Bijun and others traveled with him.

▲ Wang also telegraphed Hu Hanmin to urge him to come.

After Wang Jingwei was admitted to Rohrer Hospital, the German doctor injected him with medicine, and his condition improved slightly. Wang was urged by all parties to go to Beijing very enthusiastically in recent days. At the same time, Chiang Kai-shek replied to Wang, inviting him to Hangzhou for talks. Therefore, at 5:40 PM yesterday, he urged him to leave the hospital and go directly to Fanhuangdu Station to take the 6:20 PM train to Hangzhou to meet Chiang, expressing his active desire to serve the country. His wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, traveled with him. The details of his departure from Shanghai are recorded below:

Chen Mingshu Returns to Shanghai

Chen Mingshu, Vice President of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai at around 6 a.m. yesterday, holding Chiang Kai-shek's personal letter to Wang, accompanied by Fan Qiwu. After resting briefly at his residence, he went to Haig Road to meet Mayor Wu Tiecheng at 9 a.m. and talked for about an hour. At around 10 a.m., he went to Gu Mengyu's residence on Pushi Road and talked for about two hours. Chen left at around 12 p.m. After Chen left, Gu immediately took Chiang's letter to see Wang Jingwei and conveyed Chen Mingshu's message that Chiang hoped to invite Wang to meet him in Hangzhou. After discussion, Wang decided to leave the hospital and go to Hangzhou.

Wang Leaves Hospital

Wang ordered his family to prepare at 4 p.m. yesterday and left the hospital at 5:40 p.m. Wang wore a gray leather robe and looked listless. He was supported down the stone steps by his nephew Chen Yaozu, and then helped into the car by his wife, Chen Bijun. The reporter, seeing that Wang was going to Hangzhou while ill, did not have time to ask him in detail. After asking about his health, Wang only answered "slightly better." At that time, the car had already started. There were also two cars traveling with Wang, carrying his relatives and followers.

Fanhuangdu Station

Wang's three cars left the hospital one after another. After about fifteen minutes, they arrived at Fanhuangdu Station in West Shanghai. The 32nd Shanghai-Hangzhou night express train had not yet departed, so Wang and his wife temporarily entered the station master's office to wait. At 6:35 p.m., the Hangzhou night train arrived at the station, and Wang and others boarded the last carriage, car number P·C503, which was pre-ordered to be attached to the end of the night express train. After stopping at Fanhuangdu for about two minutes, it departed southward. It was expected to arrive at the city station at 10:15 p.m. that night.

Accompanying Family Members

In addition to his wife, Chen Bijun, those traveling with Wang yesterday included his daughter Ms. Mei Yi (transliteration), nephew Chen Yaozu, relatives Mr. Li, Mr. Liu, and others, a group of six or seven people. All of his secretaries were not in Shanghai, so none of them accompanied him.

Doctor's Talk

The reporter, seeing that Wang was suddenly going to Hangzhou, drove to Rohrer Hospital on Avenue Joffre to visit the dean, Rohrer, who kindly made the following remarks: (Question) Is it true that Mr. Wang went to Hangzhou this afternoon? (Rohrer replied) This is true. (Question) Then Mr. Wang has fully recovered from his illness? (Answer) Mr. Wang's health has generally recovered. Mr. Wang's diabetes in his salt has reached 98 points, which is no different from ordinary people, and his liver disease has also been cured by injections.

Chen Mingshu's Talk

The reporter met with Chen Mingshu yesterday. According to the talks after meeting with Chiang, Chiang expressed very well and was willing to do his best to assist the government in finances, foreign affairs, etc. Chiang also hoped that all sectors could unanimously support the government and overcome this difficulty. Moreover, I have rarely expressed any opinions to reporters in the past, but recently newspapers have said that I will do this and that in terms of finance, which is really strange. My political speeches completely set aside my military status. If I put pressure on the financial community, then why don't I use this spirit against foreigners as a revolutionary soldier? As for Chiang Kai-shek's going to Beijing, there is no problem, but I hope that no accidents will happen in Guangdong at this time, then Mr. Chiang will make a statement soon. Furthermore, as far as I know, there is no such thing as Guangdong withholding taxes.

Urge Hu to Go North Telegram

Wang telegraphed Hu Hanmin before leaving Shanghai, saying: Hong Kong China Telegraph Bureau transfers to Mr. Hu Hanmin: My brother has been sick for ten days, and he has only recently recovered slightly. During his illness, he has repeatedly received telegrams and letters from Nanjing and comrades from all parties urging my brother and others to go to Beijing to jointly overcome the national crisis and save the country. He is anxious and cannot express himself. Brother Jie has now arrived in Hangzhou and invited my brother to meet him. My brother intends to go and discuss everything. How is my brother's health recently? I miss you very much. I hope you can set off north immediately so that you can be taught in case of trouble. This telegram is to inform you and ask for a reply. Wang Zhaoming sincerely,

Telegram to Sun Ke, etc.

Another telegram to Sun Ke and others said: Nanjing Executive Yuan President Sun and Vice President Chen are both informed. My brother informed the two brothers earlier that the injection would be completed on the 10th of this month, and he could go to Beijing to recuperate. Later, due to dizziness on the 6th and 7th, the injection was stopped and extended until this morning. It has been completed. I heard that Brother Jie has come to Hangzhou, and I plan to go and meet him immediately. I hope to go to Beijing with him. First report this to you. Wang Zhaoming sincerely,

Zhang Qun's Talk

▲ The Process of Going to Hangzhou to See Chiang

Zhang Yuejun issued a statement to reporters yesterday, saying: (Reporter asked) Mr. went to Hangzhou yesterday afternoon and returned to Shanghai last night. Why are you in such a hurry? Can I hear about it? (Zhang replied) I originally wanted to stay in Hangzhou for a few days this time. Because I visited Mr. Chiang and talked about the Shanghai community's opposition to the financial policy of suspending the payment of principal and interest on domestic debt proposed by the capital, and the process of Mayor Wu's consultation with Shanghai bankers on relief. Chen, the vice president, also arrived in Hangzhou from Beijing and urged Chiang to go to Beijing. Chiang believed that the suspension of the payment of principal and interest on domestic debt would be enough to cause a national financial shock and the panic of national economic bankruptcy. However, the government's finances were in a desperate situation, and if it did not seek to save it, it would not be the way to overcome national difficulties together. The government and the banking industry groups should be based on the spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation and do their best to help the government within the scope of possibility to overcome the difficulties. He specifically asked me to rush back to Shanghai with Mr. Chen to convey this intention to the leaders of the banking industry and make it a success, so as to fulfill his responsibility to assist the government in the field. (Reporter asked) Can Mr. Chiang be bound to go to Beijing in the near future to comfort the expectations of all parties? (Zhang replied) Mr. Chiang is not impossible to go to Beijing, but because of the current environmental relationship, it is better to go there. The reason is that Mr. Chiang's remarks published in the Shanghai newspapers the day before yesterday have already explained it very clearly. At this time, going to Beijing, especially going to Beijing alone, is not only useless to the overall situation, but also gives an excuse to prevent the resurrection of dictatorship, and in fact seeks to split the agitation materials, which will only increase the disputes. Although Chiang is in the field, he will do his best to eliminate difficulties, strive to maintain, and consolidate the current unified government in Nanjing, whether he is in Beijing or not, and there are various pieces of evidence to prove it. (Reporter asked) What will Mr. do in the future? (Zhang replied) I have been exhausted recently, and I still feel overwhelmed in Shanghai. I plan to leave Shanghai temporarily in the next few days to take a rest.

▲ The Police Authorities Took Strict Precautions

Joint Announcement by Military and Political Authorities

▲ The Communist Party Has a Conspiracy to Disrupt

▲ Reiterate the Prohibition and Strictly Suppress It

The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Songhu Garrison Command issued a joint announcement yesterday, saying: To announce the matter, it has been found that since the Northeast Incident, the patriotic people of this city have been stirred by righteous indignation and have held demonstrations from time to time. However, the Communist Party and reactionaries have often been mixed in among them, resulting in numerous incidents of illegal and out-of-bounds actions. The Public Security and Social Education Bureaus have been ordered to properly persuade and suppress them. According to secret reports, the Communist Party and reactionaries have still been active recently, attempting to use the power of the masses to carry out their conspiracy of sabotage. The mayor and commander are responsible for maintaining local stability and cannot shirk their responsibility. Therefore, the prohibition is reiterated. If any lawless people disregard local security and plot to cause trouble, the mayor and commander will definitely enforce the law and punish them and will never forgive them. All patriotic people, please do not blindly follow and fall into the trap of the law. It is appropriate to announce this, and everyone must abide by it.

The Three District Party Headquarters Ask All Sectors to Carefully Consider Strikes and Stoppages

Zhonghua News Agency reported that the executive committee of the Second District Party Headquarters of this city, due to the urgent national crisis, had telegraphed the party and state leaders Wang, Chiang, and Hu to go to Beijing immediately to jointly overcome the national crisis and save the country. However, it has been reported in the newspapers in recent days that a citizens' assembly will be held in this city today and that strikes and stoppages will be advocated as a diplomatic backup. The association believes that in the autumn of foreign aggression and national crisis, these actions should be carefully considered. Therefore, it issued a declaration yesterday, saying that the invasion of Japan has made the national crisis deeper. During this period, the people of the whole country should unite as one, support the government in hard work and struggle, and cooperate sincerely to resist aggression and save the country. However, there have recently been advocates for strikes and stoppages. According to strikes and stoppages, the most painful sacrifices of the people can promote the responsibility of the authorities internally and show their weaknesses externally. For the sake of resisting aggression and violence and for the sake of the nation and the country, I deeply feel that this is not something that can be easily tried. People from all walks of life should understand the righteousness, carefully consider the situation, and clarify the advantages and disadvantages before carefully considering it in order to maintain the ambition of resisting Japan and saving the country. In addition to telegraphing the authorities to quickly save the country, this association dares to present its humble opinions and sincerely advises, hoping to be examined. (The following is omitted)

Record of the Delegates' General Assembly from Various Circles

▲Seventy-Plus Organizations Arrived

▲Multiple Important Cases Were Resolved

Due to the lack of leadership in the central government, over fifty organizations, including the National Crisis Relief Association of this port, convened a delegates' general assembly from various circles at the Sichuan Road YMCA yesterday to discuss methods for the people to defend themselves and save the nation. Over seventy organizations attended, including the National Crisis Relief Association, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, the Chinese National Crisis Relief Association, the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association, the Zhejiang General Association, the General Association of Chinese Revolutionary Students, the People's Governance Association, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of YMCA members, the West District Yarn Factory Workers' Union, and the Chinese and Western Furniture Workers' Union. The meeting lasted three hours and discussed multiple important cases, such as the people's self-defense and national salvation. The details of the assembly are recorded below:

Election of Chairmen

Around 2:00 PM, representatives of various organizations invited by the National Crisis Relief Association arrived one after another. At 2:30 PM, the meeting was declared open. After a three-minute silence to mourn the compatriots who died in the Northeast, Liu Shixiong, representative of the National Lawyers Association, Yin Zhiling, representative of the National Crisis Relief Association, Chu Fucheng, representative of the Zhejiang General Association, He Liang, representative of the People's Governance Association, and Tan Bozhi of the YMCA Aid to Ma Team were nominated as chairmen. Li Fengchu, representative of the General Association of Chinese Revolutionary Students, served as the recorder.

Chairman's Report

After the meeting commenced, Chairman Yin Zhiling reported the purpose of the meeting, stating, "Almost four months have passed since the violent Japanese invaded. Apart from protesting and requesting the League of Nations for help, the government claims to be vigorously pursuing revolutionary diplomacy and recovering lost territory in words. However, in reality, Jinzhou has recently fallen, and the situation within the country is precarious. The government, lacking a central leader, has no solution. If we, the people, are unwilling to sit and wait for our doom, we should discuss self-defense measures. Today's meeting was born out of this mission." Subsequently, Tan Bozhi and Chu Fucheng delivered their reports.

Resolution of Important Cases

The participating organizations had already submitted multiple proposals, which were compiled into ten articles by the Proposal Organizing Committee. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, discussions began, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Organize a National Automatic Convocation of the National Salvation Conference Committee; (2) Citizens should automatically organize a National Volunteer Army to cope with the national crisis; (3) Various civic organizations should supervise the anti-Japanese association and rigorously enforce economic severance; (4) Send a telegram opposing the League of Nations investigation team coming to China; (5) Send a telegram requesting the United States to convene a conference of the Nine-Power Treaty countries to protect peace in East Asia; (6) Send a telegram to He Zhuguo, the brigade commander at Shanhaiguan, pledging to resist Japan to the death; (7) Oppose warlord separatism; (8) Various civic organizations should earnestly assist the volunteer armies in various parts outside the customs; (9) Various civic organizations should quickly organize a National Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, etc.

Election of Preparatory Members

After passing the first resolution, 'Organize a National Automatic Convocation of the National Salvation Conference Committee,' the meeting immediately designated all the participating organizations as sponsors of the National Automatic Convocation of the National Salvation Conference Committee. The sponsors then mutually elected Li Fengchu of the General Association of Chinese Revolutionary Students, Weng Guoxun of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of YMCA members, Huang Jiawei of the National Anti-Drug Association, Zhao Housheng of the Chinese National Crisis Relief Association, Zhan Baichuan of the Chinese National Foreign Affairs Self-Determination Association, Zhu Shaowen of the Jiangsu National Crisis Relief Association, and the representatives of the five groups of the Presidium, totaling eleven people, as preparatory members. It is heard that after the closing of the meeting, the preparatory members held a discussion in preparation for holding a preparatory meeting soon, aiming to establish the National Automatic Convocation of the National Salvation Conference Committee in the shortest possible time.

The Executive Committee Meeting of the Anti-Japanese Federation of Civic Organizations Was Held Yesterday

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Federation of civic organizations in this city held its first Executive Committee meeting yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM at the Civic Diplomacy Support Association. The committee members present were from the Northwest Revolutionary Comrades Association, the Zhejiang Revolutionary Youth Comrades Association, the Zhejiang National Salvation Conference Promotion Association, the Shanghai College of Political Science and Law Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Shanghai Revolutionary Youth National Salvation Association, the Chinese People's Diplomacy Support Association, the Shanghai Seamen's Union, the Japanese Yarn Factory Workers' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Great China University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the Hubei Revolutionary Comrades Association, and the Gu Yan Society Anti-Japanese Association, totaling eleven organizations. Representatives from groups such as the Anhui Youth National Salvation Corps in Shanghai and the Guangdong People's National Salvation Federation in Shanghai were present as observers. (1) Liu Chuanzhong was publicly elected as chairman; (2) The meeting opened as scheduled; (3) The chairman gave a report; (4) A resolution on the distribution of duties was discussed and passed: (A) Three Standing Committee members, concurrently serving as directors of the General Affairs, Publicity, and Organization Departments. The Standing Committee member concurrently serving as the director of the General Affairs Department is from the Civic Diplomacy Support Association, the Standing Committee member concurrently serving as the director of the Publicity Department is from the Northwest Revolutionary Comrades Association, and the Standing Committee member concurrently serving as the director of the Organization Department is from the College of Political Science and Law Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association; (B) The General Affairs Department has four sections: Documentation is handled by the Zhejiang Revolutionary Youth National Salvation Association, Public Relations by the Shanghai Revolutionary Youth National Salvation Association and the Shanghai Literature and Art Research Society, Accounting by the Gu Yan Society Anti-Japanese Association, and Logistics by the Shanghai Pharmaceutical Workers' Union; (C) The Publicity Department has two sections: Publication by the Hubei Revolutionary Comrades Association and the Great China University Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, Public Speaking by the Zhejiang National Salvation Conference Promotion Association and the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army of Retired Soldiers of the Republic of China; (D) The Organization Department has two sections: Investigation by the Japanese-owned Yarn Factory Workers' National Salvation Association and Registration by the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Anti-Japanese Association. The meeting received the resolution of the delegates' general assembly, telegraphed Wang Jingwei, Chiang Kai-shek, and Hu Hanmin to come to Beijing together to face the national crisis, sent a telegram of condolence to the anti-Japanese generals and volunteer armies in the Northeast, sent a circular to the people nationwide to quickly organize volunteer armies, sent a circular to the already organized volunteer armies nationwide to depart for the anti-Japanese front immediately, and issued a declaration. It was resolved to hand these over to the Standing Committee for handling. A draft outline of the work of each department was discussed and resolved to be drafted quickly by each department and submitted to the next Executive Committee meeting for approval. The investigation of civic organizations in Shanghai was resolved to be handled by the Organization Department. The organization of an Economic Committee was resolved, approved, and entrusted to the directors of the three departments and the Shanghai Revolutionary Youth National Salvation Association and the Shanghai Seamen's Union to organize it. The determination of the meeting time and address of the committee was resolved to be held every Wednesday at 1:00 PM at the Civic Diplomacy Committee. It was decided to hold an Anti-Japanese Propaganda Week on a regular basis and hand it over to the Publicity Department for handling. The resolution to send a circular to the people nationwide to unanimously arm themselves and declare war on Japan was handed over to the Standing Committee for handling. The resolution to send a telegram to the government requesting it to announce its policy towards Japan was handed over to the Standing Committee for handling. The meeting was adjourned.

Sheng Minxiu Telegraphed Encouragement to He Zhuguo

In view of the escalating aggression by the violent Japanese and the successive retreats of our troops in Jinzhou and Suiyuan, He Zhuguo, the commander of the Second Brigade of the Northeast Border Defense Army, had expressed his determination to defend Shanhaiguan and fulfill his military duty while governing the army at Luan River. Sheng Minxiu (former advisor to the Central Route Army during the anti-Russian war), an old friend of He's in Shanghai, specially sent a telegram of consolation yesterday. The original telegram is recorded below: "Commander He Zhuguo, distinguished merit: In the summer of the eighteenth year, I wandered in Jin, Yi, and Chaoyang. You did not abandon He Fei, and I gathered information from you. I secretly admired you greatly. Later, when the Sino-Russian Incident occurred, I, with the feeling of treating the symptoms in an emergency, served as an advisor to the Central Route Army, followed Brother Chu (Huang Shiyue)'s army to Jiang. When I arrived at Nenjiang, the military situation was tense. The Central Route Army only had two brigades, Huang and Ma. Through Brother Chu's introduction, I met General Ma Zhanshan. At that time, his troops numbered only over three thousand, but their morale was high. Although Russia was arrogant, it did not dare to invade. How long has it been since the September 18th Incident occurred and the Northeast fell? Compatriots across the country were indignant and wanted to die. However, General Ma defended with a lone army and defended the country with loyalty and courage. Although he could not protect the territory for a while, his military might shocked the bandits. From then on, he shone brightly in the world, and I was fortunate to know him. I originally intended to pack my bags and go east, but because I was in Shanghai, I devoted myself to social work, only making propaganda to save the country, so that those who defend the country would be more successful. For the past two weeks, Jinzhou has fallen again, and Shanhaiguan is in danger again. Knowing that you are guarding the Luan River and protecting this remnant fortress, I predict that you will be the one to rise up after General Ma Zhanshan. I regret that I have received little military training in my life and find it difficult to wield a weapon and defend the country. However, I have a responsibility for the rise and fall of the nation. I plan to come north, hoping to offer some small assistance. I hope that you will maintain your consistent personality of matching words with actions, firmly defend Yuguan. The bandits may be fierce, but they will never be able to shake the soldiers touched by our sincerity. 'The city falls with us,' is an ancient saying. You have been in the military since you were young. If you can understand this, then someone as mediocre as I will have no more regrets. It is bitterly cold outside the pass. I pray that you will cherish your health for the sake of the country. My mind races as I write this telegram, and I cannot express all my thoughts. Sincerely, Sheng Minxiu."

The Life Weekly's Announcement of the End of the Aid-to-Ma Donation Campaign

▲Total Amount Reached Over 125,000 Yuan

Since the Life Weekly initiated a campaign to raise funds to assist the patriotic soldiers in Heilongjiang Province, it has been trusted by people from all walks of life at home and abroad, who have enthusiastically donated and entrusted remittances. As of January 15th, the total amount received was 125,454.53 yuan. Of this amount, 106,507 yuan has already been received by General Ma (the receipts for each donation were specially made with copperplate and published in the magazine). Another 13,500 yuan is being processed for delivery through a bank in Harbin, and 5,447.53 yuan remains in the Shanghai bank. It is now learned that the magazine received a telegram from General Ma on January 5th from Hailun, stating that the current military pay is still self-sufficient and requesting that remittances be stopped to help the disaster victims. Therefore, it was decided to end the aid-to-Ma donation campaign on January 16th. Apart from continuing to remit the remaining funds that have already been donated and designated for aid to Ma in order to fulfill the donors' intentions, only disaster relief donations will be accepted in the future, and no more aid-to-Ma donations will be accepted for the time being. Furthermore, for the sake of ensuring the integrity of the various account books and receipts for this aid-to-Ma donation campaign, accountant Pan Xulun will be invited to audit them after the campaign is concluded and issue a certificate to be published in the magazine to complete the procedures.

Order of the National Government to Investigate the Organization of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions

▲The Municipal Government Orders the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus to Handle It

▲Tomorrow, the Committee Members of the Federation of Trade Unions Will Be Summoned for Talks

In order to unite the labor circles of this city and seek the vital interests of the workers, the Postal Workers' Union and others convened a delegates' congress of trade unions and established the Shanghai Special Municipality Federation of Trade Unions. The Publishing Workers' Union and others convened a delegates' congress of trade unions and established the Shanghai Municipal Federation of Trade Unions. Later, the full committees of the North and South Municipal Federations of Trade Unions held a meeting and merged into the Shanghai Federation of Trade Unions, using No. 9 Runde Lane, Fusheng Road, Zhabei as the address. The Municipal Government believes that the organization of the Federation of Trade Unions has no legal basis and submitted a request to the Central Government for instructions on how to handle it. The Central Government then forwarded it to the National Government for handling. The Municipal Government received an order from the National Government, relayed by the Central Government, a few days ago, stating that the establishment of the North and South Municipal Federations of Trade Unions should be investigated and prevented in order to maintain the law and discipline and prevent disputes. Mayor Wu Tiecheng immediately instructed the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus to handle it jointly. The director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Mai Chaochu, summoned the committee members of the Federation of Trade Unions, Li Yongxiang, Zhu Xuefan, Chen Haiqiu, Ge Hecai, Yang Youren, Chen Peide, Ge Yunting, Yu Xianting, etc., for talks after receiving the order. The notification letter is recorded below: "Notification regarding the establishment of the Federation of Trade Unions in this city. This bureau has scheduled a discussion for 10:00 AM on January 18th. You are hereby notified to come to the bureau on time to attend the discussion. Sincerely, January 16th, the 21st year of the Republic of China."

Upon review, the Merchant Movement Committee has no legal basis and has been ordered to be stopped by the Executive Yuan.
