Late-Night Curfew at the South Railway Station

▲Passengers Are Not Allowed to Pass Through the Platform

▲Passengers Feel Deeply Inconvenienced

Guomin News reports that a curfew has been implemented at the South Railway Station every night recently. Even train passengers are not allowed to pass through the platform. The 33rd express train arrived at the station around 10:00 PM on the 15th, with many passengers. It was during the curfew hours, and passengers were not allowed to pass through the platform. Even after negotiations by the station staff, it was to no avail. As a result, all the passengers had to cross the tracks to exit the station. Passengers with more luggage were complaining endlessly, and female passengers felt particularly embarrassed. It is reported that the reason for the curfew is that the headquarters and the entire Third Battalion of the 19th Regiment of the 10th Brigade of the 4th Division, led by Regiment Commander and Acting Brigade Commander Ma Liwu, arrived in Shanghai from Jiangxi, with about 400-500 officers and soldiers. They are stationed on the train and will be waiting to board a ship to travel to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River in a few days.

The Strike at the Cloth Weaving Section of the Japanese-Owned China Cotton Mill Was Resolved with a Breakdown in Mediation

▲The Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus Reported to the Municipal Government for Review

After all the workers in the cloth weaving section of the Japanese-owned China Cotton Mill in Pudong went on strike, the Japanese used force to prevent them from returning to work. Despite repeated mediation by the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus, the mediation broke down due to the Japanese side's strong attitude. They reported to the Municipal Government for review. The workers, with no avenue for appeal and facing a precarious livelihood, had no choice but to convene another general assembly at the trade union at 10:00 AM yesterday to discuss solutions. Chairman Zheng Xiechen: (1) Regarding the matter of how to handle the failure of the Social Affairs Bureau to negotiate with the seller on several occasions regarding the cloth weaving section turmoil, it was resolved to petition the Social Affairs Bureau for review again and to send representatives Huang Linxiang and Wang Haiqing, etc., to petition. (2) Regarding the matter of the employer canceling the monthly bonus for no reason and illegally dismissing a large number of workers, it was resolved to handle it in conjunction with item 1. (3) Regarding how to handle the contractor of the carrying-pole section violating the contract, it was resolved to send a letter ordering the contractor to submit the original prices for verification. (4) Regarding the request to punish the female yarn gatherer for fawning over the employer and forcibly confiscating the trade union certificates of female workers, it was resolved to send a letter ordering the association to severely reprimand her. (5) Regarding the prevention of female workers from collecting monthly fees for assisting workers in other sections by patrol police from the Fourth Squad while they are advising them outside the cloth weaving section, it was resolved to send a letter to the Third District Public Security Bureau to notify the Fourth Squad not to interfere. (6) Regarding the request to finalize the liquidation accounts for the December 20th year of the Republic of China and to publish the list, it was resolved to finalize and publish the list by the 30th of this month. (7) Regarding how to handle the trade union's financial difficulties, it was resolved to send a letter to the trade unions in Pudong requesting them to send representatives to the meeting for discussion. (8) Regarding the inconvenience for trade union members to enter and exit the trade union building, it was resolved to move to the building opposite the Great Pudong Theater. (9) Regarding Comrade Zheng Xiechen's letter of resignation from the position of permanent secretary due to poor health, it was unanimously resolved to retain him.

The Japanese Cotton Mills' Response to the Monthly Bonus Labor Unrest

▲An Emergency Meeting of Representatives Was Held Yesterday

▲The Secret Meeting Adopted a Tough Stance

▲Unemployed Japanese Workers Are Likely to Come to Shanghai

Since over 30 Japanese-owned cotton mills in this city, including Rihua, employing over 60,000 Chinese workers, aroused a full-scale strike after the factories unilaterally canceled the monthly bonus, several days have passed without a solution. While the Japanese cotton mills are superficially maintaining a calm attitude, they are actually panicked. Since the East Incident occurred, our country, both from top to bottom, has been vigorously boycotting Japanese goods. The cotton textile industry in our port has been replacing Japanese raw materials with British goods. Japanese products are temporarily unable to sell, and the business has indeed suffered a drastic blow. By today, the inventory of each factory has gradually been sold out, and the business has slightly improved. However, the Japanese factories have always adopted a high-pressure policy towards Chinese workers. Therefore, after the occurrence of this strike, our party and government agencies sent personnel for mediation several times, but were rejected by the Japanese side. The conditions proposed by the workers have not been accepted. On the other hand, representatives from all Shanghai yarn factories were summoned to hold a joint meeting to find a fundamental solution. It has been learned that the Japanese Cotton Mills Association in China, seeing the increasingly serious situation of the Chinese workers' strikes in various factories recently, is discussing countermeasures, and no time can be lost. It specially convened an emergency joint meeting of representatives from various factories at 8:00 PM last night, which continued until 11:00 PM without adjourning. When the representatives of the Japanese cotton mills held the meeting, plainclothes Japanese were densely deployed around the meeting place. Only representatives with official certificates from the factory were allowed to enter. All others were uniformly refused to eavesdrop. Therefore, the content of the meeting is unknown. However, according to another source from the Japanese side, it is said that the emergency meeting will adopt a tough stance on the Chinese workers' strike events in various factories, insisting to the end and refusing to accept mediation from any party. If the Chinese workers do not return to work at the factories within the next ten days, their back wages will be settled, and they will be dismissed. Other Chinese workers will be recruited to supplement them. If Chinese workers cannot be recruited temporarily, workers from other countries or Japanese workers will be recruited as much as possible to temporarily maintain operations. At the same time, a telegram was sent urgently to the Osaka Textile Committee in China, requesting them to find ways to recruit a large number of unemployed Japanese people to come to Shanghai quickly to replace the work of Chinese workers.

Local News II

Statistics of the Two Courts in the Special District Last Year

▲ Totaling 104,190 Cases

Last year, the Provisional Court of the First Special District of Shanghai, together with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, heard a total of 104,190 cases. Of the accused, those found guilty accounted for 91.4 percent. The previous year, a total of 97,665 cases were heard, with those found guilty accounting for 93.1 percent. Last year, 23,624 major and minor criminal cases were completely litigated, resulting in 21,586 convictions and 2,030 acquittals. Furthermore, no fewer than 69,612 individuals forfeited their bail due to failing to appear in court after being charged with violating the regulations of the Public Works Department. In addition, there were 1,237 criminal cases initiated by victims themselves, 2,193 cases of violations prosecuted by the Health Department and the Public Works Department, and 7,206 cases of traffic violations. A total of 314 cases were withdrawn due to insufficient evidence. As for appeals, there were 475 cases, of which 319 upheld the original verdict, 13 were remanded for retrial, 51 had their sentences reduced, 7 had their sentences increased, 50 appellants were acquitted, and 35 appeals were withdrawn.

A Glimpse of the Current Situation of Flood Victims in Wuhan

▲ Crying for Food, Unable to Find Work

▲ Without Proper Relief, Reduced Entirely to Vagrants

The National Association of the Young Women's Christian Association (YWCA) Disaster Relief Committee specially dispatched two female officers, Tian Cuibao and Wang Fuying, to the disaster areas in Wuhan at the end of September last year to provide on-the-ground services. It has now been learned that Ms. Tian returned to Shanghai from Hongshan, Wuchang, the day before yesterday to report on the situation. According to her, there are over ten thousand flood victims residing in shelters in Wuhan. Since November 10 of last year, the Hubei Provincial Emergency Relief Association has ceased operations, and the porridge kitchens and temporary hospitals operated by various organizations have also gradually closed, causing widespread panic among the flood victims. Subsequently, the Emergency Relief Association issued five sheng of rice to each flood victim, ordering them to return to their hometowns. However, the flood victims still did not leave. Therefore, the Flood Relief Committee issued six jin of flour and a set of cotton clothing to each person. Recently, local philanthropists have provided each person with one sheng of rice and five jin of flour. Therefore, the flood victims are constantly at risk of starvation. However, the Relief Committee has established women and children's shelters in Wuchang, Hankou, and Hanyang, each capable of accommodating 2,000 people. A small number of philanthropists have also established children's shelters and orphanages in Wuchang, all of which have already reached their capacity of 500 children. As for the YWCA's shelter for orphans and the elderly in Hongshan, it is the first pilot shelter for orphans and the elderly in Wuhan. The shelter uses the Baotong Temple as its address. In addition to nurses, there are ten other staff members, all of whom are YWCA officers. Unfortunately, the shelter can only accommodate 300 orphaned and elderly flood victims. The remaining over 90,000 flood victims are unable to return to their hometowns and lack sufficient food to stay warm. Most pitiable is that diseases such as smallpox, measles, and dysentery are still prevalent. However, in Hongshan, for example, there are only three nurses for over 10,000 flood victims, and they are crying for food all day long, unable to find work. Cases of women selling themselves are frequently heard of. If this continues without proper relief measures, then these over 90,000 flood victims will all become vagrants.

Rice Industry Discusses Using New Measuring Instruments

The Shanghai Soy and Rice Trade Association, the Rice Shop Trade Association, the Rice Milling Industry Association, the Nanshi Rice Merchants Association, and the Changshu Rice Merchants Association, etc., previously received orders to abolish all previous weights and measures and adopt the weights and measures of Shanghai Municipality as stipulated by the authorities. The associations have been rushing to produce dozens of city hu, city dou, city sheng, and other measures and have submitted them to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Weights and Measures for inspection and approval before distributing them to their members for use. In order to schedule the implementation of this matter, the associations specially dispatched representatives to hold a joint meeting at Cuixiu Hall at around 2:00 PM yesterday. After the temporary chairman, Zhu Zixiang, reported the purpose of the meeting, the old-style Haihu and the city hu were compared in terms of weight, and then a lengthy discussion was held. It was then decided that from February 10, 1932, all members of the associations would uniformly adopt the new-style city weights and measures. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Chicken and Duck Shops on the Bund Restricted to Relocate to Dongjiadu Within One Month

▲ Joint Notice from the Municipal Public Security Bureau and the County Finance Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and the County Finance Bureau jointly notified the chicken and duck shops, stating that the Bund area is prosperous with bustling traffic and many pedestrians. The chicken and duck shops along the road obstruct traffic and sanitation. The Public Security Bureau has repeatedly ordered the first district in charge to strictly ban them. The County Finance Bureau has also stipulated that when the chicken and duck shops in the area renew their licenses, those with housing facilities must obtain a shop guarantee to ensure that chicken and duck cages are not placed along the road. Those who violate this will be punished before being granted a license. Open-air vendors will not be allowed to pay for licenses in order to rectify the situation and benefit traffic. Recently, it was found that 18 chicken and duck shops, including Yitaifeng, still placed chicken and duck cages along the road for open-air business, which is inappropriate. Therefore, Yitaifeng and other 18 chicken and duck shops are notified to relocate to a suitable location south of Dongjiadu within one month of receiving this notice, otherwise their licenses will be revoked and they will be ordered to close down in order to serve as a warning to others. You must abide by this. This notice is given to the chicken and duck shops on the [day] of January, 21st year of the Republic of China.

Director Wen Yingxing, Director Wang Huazhao.

Theft of Over 20,000 Taels of Raw Silk

▲ Hidden in the Home of Wang Yanchun

▲ The Case Was Tried and a Fine Was Imposed

The Ruilun Silk Factory, located at No. 217 Feilun Road, had 12 bundles of raw silk worth 27,000 taels of silver stolen between the 26th of last month. The case was reported to the Hongkou Police Department. Later, Chinese Detective Shi Deyu discovered that the stolen goods were hidden in the home of Wang Yanchun, a Hangzhou native, at No. 10 Yide Lane, Linyin Road, in the Chinese area of Nanshi. He secretly went with detectives from the Public Security Bureau there, arrested Wang, and learned that a portion of the original stolen goods had been sent to Ma Hanru, a native of Changzhou, a friend at the Xilin Temple on Xilin Road. They immediately went to the address, apprehended Ma, and brought back the stolen silk in three wooden boxes to the Police Department, and sent them to the First Special District Court for interrogation and detention. The stolen goods were first returned to the owner. Yesterday, Judge Jiang presided over a continued interrogation in the Third Criminal Court. Police Lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the case and questioned Wang Yanchun. Wang confessed that the silk belonged to a Zhang surname, his tenant, who said that he intended to open a sock factory and that the silk came from the sale of mortgaged goods from a certain Qianzhuang [money exchange]. He said that he knew Ma, so he temporarily sent the goods there. He said that he did not know that it was stolen goods and that the Zhang surname had already fled. Ma Hanru confessed that on the 27th of last month, Wang Yanchun delivered three wooden boxes of silk, saying that they were materials for his tenant, the Zhang surname, to weave socks, and that they would be taken away in a few days. He did not suspect that they were stolen goods of unknown origin. He asked the court for clarification and hired lawyer Fan Gang for his defense. Judge Jiang, after hearing the arguments of both lawyers, sentenced Wang Yanchun to a fine of 240 yuan and acquitted Ma Hanru. Police Lawyer Qian abandoned the appeal for Ma Hanru and released him in court.

Another Embezzlement Lawsuit Arises in the Housheng Bonus Case

▲ Jiang Zhonghe and Four Others Accused

▲ Plaintiff Must Supplement Procedures

Seven shareholders and directors of the Housheng Ziji Yarn Factory in Yangshupu, including Bei Runsheng and Xue Gansheng, were criminally prosecuted by representatives of the factory's employees, Jiang Zhonghe, Sun Kezhen, Xu Dianhuang, and Zhou Qichang, last winter for embezzling hundreds of thousands of dollars in dividends over the years (from 1926 to 1929) in the First Special District Court. Judge Feng interrogated them several times without a conclusion. Later, the matter was settled through mediation for 59,000 yuan. After deducting mediation fees, legal fees, and all other expenses, the net amount was only 43,000 yuan. The employees, believing that they were entitled to more than 100,000 yuan, sued Jiang Zhonghe and the other three for fraud and breach of trust in the original court, Yesterday afternoon, Judge Xiao Xieben specially opened the Fifth Criminal Court to summon the defendants. The plaintiffs' representatives, Li Bo, Ying Chengzong, Xing Haoqi, and Li Jingfu, were chosen. Li Bo stated that during the litigation, at a meeting at the Central Hotel on Guangdong Road, it was said that at least 100,000 yuan or more must be obtained. This statement was made by Zhou Qichang, and the goal must be achieved. Unexpectedly, the result of the mediation was only 43,000 yuan net, which was far less than the expected amount. Please investigate. The defendant Jiang Zhonghe confessed that during the case, they were indeed chosen as representatives, and after a detailed investigation of the accounts, the amount that should have been obtained was no more than 59,000 yuan. After deducting the fees of the mediators Ma Changshu and Tang Jiapeng and lawyer fees of 16,000 yuan, the remaining amount should be distributed to the employees, and 130 people have already received it. Only 80 people have not received it. Furthermore, the funds from the factory were transferred by Ma and Tang. The confessions of the defendants Sun and Xu were the same. Zhou Qichang denied that he had said at the Central Hotel that 100,000 yuan or more must be obtained. Judge Xiao ordered the four defendants, including Jiang, to provide reliable shop guarantees, and ordered the plaintiffs to supplement the power of attorney procedures, and then set another date for further interrogation.

Pengpu Militia Captures a Giant Thief Who Climbs Walls

▲ Escaped Twice after Being Handcuffed, Finally Captured

At around 6:00 PM the day before yesterday, a thief was stealing lead sheets on the roof of the newly built Daxing Grocery Market at the intersection of Zhongxing Road and Datong Road in Zhabei. His method was to roll the entire new lead sheet into a roll like a bolt of cloth, and then carry it away to flee. This was probably not the first time. A member of the Pengpu Militia watching over the construction site discovered this, went forward to question him. The thief replied that he was a laborer. The militia member, knowing that it was theft, pretended not to notice and retreated, secretly reporting to the Second Team headquarters, and called a foreman, Mr. Jia, to assist several militia members in going to the scene. The thief was still seriously rolling up the lead sheets. Jia identified that he was not a laborer, so they arrested him and took him to the team headquarters. According to the interrogation, he confessed that his name was Chuan San, 26 years old, from Tongzhou, living at No. 3 Sanyili, Pushan Road. He has a 59-year-old mother, Yang, and an elder brother, Chuan Yi, 33 years old, and a second elder brother, Chuan Er, 28 years old, who all live by farming. He came to Shanghai more than a year ago and made a living by stealing. He has two scars on his right shoulder, which he said were marks from carrying salt illegally when he was at home, but they looked like knife scars. The team planned to send him to the vagrant factory, but the thief was very strong and could not be subdued by a small number of team members, so his hands were handcuffed to prevent accidents. However, the thief acted as if nothing had happened. At around 10:00 PM, he took advantage of the inattentiveness of others, stole the key, took off the handcuffs, and tried to escape. He was noticed by someone and relocked. This morning at around 2:00 AM, the team members were all asleep, with only one night watchman on duty at the door. The thief actually took off the handcuffs, escaped to the eaves of the building, jumped to the opposite wall to the entrance of the alley, saw someone on guard, jumped into the courtyard of No. 1 resident, and accidentally broke a flower pot in the dark, making a loud noise. Someone shouted for help, and he was captured again by the team. Yesterday, he was sent to the vagrant work practice center but was not accepted. He is still being held at the team headquarters, and it is unknown how to dispose of him. Yesterday, seeing that the thief's clothes were tattered and his eyes were sideways, everyone called him a giant of thieves.

Child Dies After Taking Medicine, Doctor Accused

Zhang Tingzhen, 47 years old, a native of Yanzhou, Shandong, residing at No. 47 Chongxin Workshop, Caojiadu, West Shanghai, worked as a factory worker. He had a son named Wu Jing, only ten years old, who was clever and loved by his father. However, the child had suffered from vomiting since childhood, sometimes recurring and sometimes recovering, so his body was very weak. Recently, due to the cold weather, the old illness recurred and was even more severe than before. His father, Tingzhen, specially invited Dr. Wang Dianchen, who lived at No. 1500 Jisi Fei Er Road, to his home for a diagnosis on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Wang immediately prescribed a prescription of three liang of licorice powder, a bottle of heart-pain pills, and two flavors of Maoshu and cloves to be decocted in soup and taken. Zhang Tingzhen took the prescription to the Gongjitang Pharmacy in the town to purchase the medicine, brought it home, and immediately prepared it and administered it. Unexpectedly, the child took half a dose of the medicine and, at around 10:00 PM, suddenly suffered from abdominal pain, gasped, and became congested. By the time the sky was about to break, he died. Tingzhen believed that the child's death was obviously caused by the quack doctor's murder and the wrong medicine. Yesterday morning, Tingzhen brought the medicine and evidence to the police station, arrested Dr. Wang Dianchen and Shi Yongsheng, a worker at the Gongjitang Pharmacy, and took them back to the Sixth District Police Station, requesting interrogation. After District Chief Ren interrogated the plaintiff Zhang Tingzhen and recorded the above statement, Dr. Wang Dianchen, 67 years old, a native of Qingfeng, Hebei, residing on Jisi Fei Er Road, admitted to prescribing the medicines. Shi Yongsheng, 26 years old, a native of Yangzhou, claimed that he gave the medicine according to the prescription and there was no mistake. After obtaining the confessions, District Chief Ren believed that the case involved accusations against the doctor for prescribing the wrong medicine and causing death, and he immediately prepared a document and sent it to the local court for interrogation.

Zhong Zhangyao's Concubine-Taking Dispute Is Full of Troubles

▲ Sometimes Gang Up for Intimidation, Sometimes Send Warning Letters

▲ Sometimes Bring Civil Lawsuits, Making It Difficult to Grasp

Chen Xiuying, a woman from Huzhou, Zhejiang, is 22 years old this year. When she was young, her mother betrothed her to Fan Dayong, a fellow villager, as his wife. Fan works in the military and is stationed in Han Gao. Due to his occupation, he has not yet discussed marriage. Unexpectedly, on May 18 of last year, Chen Xiuying suddenly changed her name to Ruizhi. Through the introduction of a woman named Shen Peizhen, she suddenly married Zhong Zhangyao as his concubine. On the 27th of that month, she changed her name to Jingfang and posted a notice in the newspaper warning her fiancé Fan Dayong. Fan saw the notice in the newspaper in Han and rushed to Shanghai to negotiate. At the same time, Fan's mother, Jiang, sued Zhong in the First Special Court for adultery. Subsequently, Zhong Zhangyao was acquitted. Fan then filed a lawsuit to confirm the marriage contract. While the lawsuit was in progress, Chen Xiuying suddenly ran away from Zhong's house and hired a lawyer to warn Zhong. Zhong carefully considered the situation and believed that there was a conspiracy to defraud him of money in the previous events. Therefore, he hired lawyers Xu Bingcheng and Xu Fuji to file a criminal complaint with the First Court against Chen Xiuying, Fan Dayong, Fan's mother Jiang, and Chen's mother, accusing them of conspiracy to defraud him of money. The reason was that Ruizhi (i.e., Xiuying) claimed after entering the house that her ex-husband was Jin Baimin and that she had a son, but because both her husband and son had died, she had no way to survive and had to remarry. However, within ten days, she came up with a whimsical idea, changed her name to Jingfang, and posted a notice in the newspaper warning her fiancé Fan Dayong to come to discuss the matter as soon as possible. Fan soon came and asked Zhong to compensate him for his losses, at least 2,000 yuan. Zhong entrusted a lawyer to pay the money and break off the engagement with Fan. Unexpectedly, they then ganged up to file a criminal complaint, which failed. Then they filed a civil lawsuit against Chen, requesting confirmation of the marriage contract. Zhong ignored it. Seeing that their purpose could not be achieved, Chen Ruizhi swept away the jewelry and ran away. Moreover, she hired a lawyer to warn Zhong, and the lawyer they hired was Huang Xiubo, Fan Dayong's agent. Shanghai, located in a corner, is a gathering place for all evils, so fraud is rampant, setting up scams and releasing pigeons. It happens almost every day. However, Chen Ruizhi's various behaviors, sometimes ganging up for intimidation, sometimes sending warning letters, sometimes bringing criminal lawsuits, and sometimes bringing civil lawsuits, not only make it impossible for people to grasp, but also make people exhausted to deal with them. She has the means of a god. Her design is ingenious, and her intentions are sinister, which is very different from the general pigeon releasers. If she is not severely punished according to the law, the harm to society in the future will be unimaginable. It is requested that the defendants be punished with the punishment they deserve according to Article 363 of the Criminal Law, and that the clothing and other losses be recovered. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Jiang Gongliang opened the court to summon the defendants. First, Zhong Zhangyao and his agent lawyer Xu Bingcheng stated the intent of the prosecution. Chen Xiuying confessed that she was still young when her parents betrothed her to Fan Dayong, so she did not know about it. Last year, she came to Shanghai and wanted to work in a silk factory but failed. Through the introduction of Shen Peizhen, she married Zhong as his wife. At that time, it was made clear that she was to be a stepmother, but unexpectedly she was a concubine. However, what is done cannot be undone. Judge Jiang believed that the case required the summon of the matchmaker Shen Peizhen, so he ordered that the case be adjourned for another hearing.

Imprisonment for Falsely Claiming Official Status to Extort Money

▲ Zhang, Tong, and Qiu Each Sentenced to One Year in Prison

Zhang Jifu, Tong Jianzhong, and Qiu Yaoshan obtained a forged white silk letter of appointment from Zheng Guoping, a native of Taizhou, stating that Wu Zhuowei, a division commander of the Fourth Group Army of Guangdong, appointed Qian Jingren as deputy brigade commander. At 9:00 AM on December 14 of last year, they gathered a group to the home of Wu Zhuohui (i.e., Zhuowei), a native of Jinhua and former captain of the Liang-Zhe Anti-Smuggling Brigade, at No. 1 Lianyifang, Xiafei Road, French Concession, accusing Wu of posing as a division commander and issuing letters of appointment indiscriminately. They claimed that the National Government had offered a reward of 5,000 yuan for his arrest. At the time, Zhang posed as a detective from the French Concession, and Qiu posed as a detective from the Siyu Department. They told Wu that the National Government had official business with the Jiangsu Security Team, which would transfer it to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for the French Concession police to assist in the arrest. If he could pay 2,000 yuan, they could find a way to let him escape. Wu did not have money at home, so he invited his friend Hu Shuang to borrow 100 yuan, which he paid first, and agreed to pay the rest the following afternoon. At 10:00 AM on the 16th, Zhang and the other two went to Wu's place to collect the money. Wu notified the Guanlong Police Station and reported to the French Concession Police Station. Detectives Liu Jinrong and Miao Yongxing went to arrest Zhang and the other two, sent them to the Second Special District Court for interrogation and detention, and then arrested Zheng Guoping, retrieved the forged letter of appointment, and sent them to the Court Police Station for prosecution on charges of extortion under Article 370 of the Criminal Law. The case was previously reported. Judge Luo Renji repeatedly held court hearings. The defendants, except for Zheng Guoping, who hired a lawyer to represent him, were assigned pro bono lawyers by the court. After the debate was declared over, the date for sentencing was set. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. At 10:00 AM, Judge Luo presided over the First Criminal Court, ordered the defendants to be brought to court, and sentenced Zhang Jifu, Tong Jianshan, and Qiu Yaoshan to one year of imprisonment each for the crime of jointly using their illegal actions to extort the possessions of another through intimidation. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be two days offsetting one day of imprisonment. Zheng Guoping was acquitted.

Sentencing for Forcibly Taking Over a Trade Union

Li Changgui, Zhang Tingsheng, Li Menggeng, and others, on the morning of December 21st of last year, under the name of the Shanghai Special Municipality Workers' Sports Committee, led a mob of over thirty people, wielding iron bars and other weapons, and stormed into the Pudong Fifth District Cigarette Industry Union, intending to forcibly take it over. Unexpectedly, the union had been forewarned and was well-prepared, resulting in Li and others being ambushed and captured on the spot. They were transferred to the Third District Police Station and then handed over to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Subsequently, the other followers were deemed to be uninvolved and were ordered to be released. The principal culprits in the case, Li and the other two, were transferred to the local court. After repeated hearings, a verdict has been announced: Li Changgui, Zhang Tingsheng, and Li Menggeng were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of publicly gathering a crowd to use violence and intimidation to assist in the takeover; and each fined fifty yuan for the crime of jointly damaging the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, to be executed concurrently. If the fines were not paid after compulsory execution, they would be converted to imprisonment at the rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention prior to the final judgment would be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The five long and short iron bars and three badges were confiscated.

The Eurasia Air Route to Be Realized in March

▲ Board of Directors to Meet Soon to Discuss Everything

The Shanghai-Berlin Eurasia air route has been actively pursued since the successful trial flight of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation on the Northwest route. The Northwest route's operability means that the route from Shanghai to Berlin can pass through the Northwest, entering Russia and then Germany. According to sources from the company yesterday, the board of directors is scheduled to meet soon to decide on the purchase of aircraft for the Northwest route from Germany and to discuss the official flight date. It is currently anticipated that the route can be opened in March of this spring. The route will be from Shanghai to Dihua in Xinjiang, from Dihua to Tacheng on the border with Russia, and then from Tacheng across the Russian border to Berlin. It is estimated that the journey between Shanghai and Berlin will only take five to six days, which is much faster than the route through Manchuria, Irkutsk, and into Germany.

Maintaining Commercial Transportation on the Yangtze River Line

▲ Reduced Load and Increased Freight Rates

▲ Navigation Marks and Lightships Remain Open

▲ The Great Recession of River Water: During last year's major flood in Wuhan, sand and mud on both banks of the Yangtze River were washed away and subsided, accumulating at the bottom of the river. Since winter, the river water has receded sharply, resulting in an unprecedented drought. The water level in the Xun and Wan sections is only above nine feet. Yesterday, a telegram from Hankou stated that the water level had dropped to eight feet seven inches, making it impossible for large river steamers to pass.

▲ Customs Erects Marks: At Taiziji in the lower reaches of Anqing, many commercial vessels were stranded due to the receding river water, numbering as many as seven. It has now slightly increased to ten feet. In order to maintain traffic on the Yangtze River, the Jianghai Customs has dispatched survey vessels to the area to erect markers in shallow waters, allowing river steamers to avoid them. Marker lights are added at night to prevent them from mistakenly entering shallow waters again. This has already been implemented.

▲ Scheduled Vessels Not Suspended: After the river steamers were pulled out of the shallows and sailed to Hankou, in view of the fact that the river water could not rise immediately, the Sanbei, Fengpu, Xinning, Xing and other vessels sent telegrams to Shanghai to inquire whether the general office would suspend scheduled services and wait for the water to rise before resuming operations. Yesterday, it was heard that the companies had agreed that the scheduled vessels would not be suspended no matter how shallow the water was. It was also agreed that vessels going up and down the river would only be allowed to load up to 40% of their capacity. It is feared that many merchants will be delayed.

Page 16

Continued Increase in Water Freight Rates

The Yangtze River shipping companies had already agreed to increase shallow water freight rates by 15% from the 16th of last month. However, at that time, it was only limited to goods going to the ports of Gou and Han in the upper reaches, while Anqing, Wuhu, and other places were not increased. Now, due to the decline in water levels in both the upper and lower reaches, the companies held another meeting yesterday and decided to revise the previously set shallow water freight rates. Starting tomorrow, the previously increased 15% will be cancelled, and the shallow water freight rate for goods transported from Shanghai to Jiujiang and Hankou will be increased by 30%. After the public discussion and decision yesterday, a notice was issued to all passengers and merchants.

Ye Xiasheng Advocates Improving National Defense Organization

According to the Guowen News Agency, Ye Xiasheng, a former National Assembly member of the Kuomintang, issued a telegram yesterday advocating the improvement of national defense organization. The original text is as follows: To the members of the Central Party Headquarters of Nanjing, the Chairman of the National Government, all members, the heads of all ministries and commissions, the military and civilian officials of the capital and various provinces, all legal entities, all newspapers, all celebrities out of office, Mr. Wang Jingwei of Shanghai, Ms. Soong Ching Ling, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek of Fenghua, Mr. Hu Hanmin of Hong Kong, Mr. Yan Xichuan of Taiyuan, Mr. Feng Huanzhang of Nanjing, Mr. Zhang Hanqing of Beiping, and Mr. Ma Zhanshan of Hailun, for your consideration. Since the national crisis occurred, all of us commoners, and even patriotic compatriots, have been hoping that the authorities will analyze the situation and adapt accordingly, and make plans as soon as possible. Gu Weijun, the Ningyue government, all regard unified national salvation and decide on the success or failure of peace negotiations. Fortunately, a government of united and unanimous opposition to foreign countries has been established. However, the political structure has three commissions, but it has not yet entered the capital, and the special affairs committee has also been organized. The veteran heroes are the pillars of the country, and they need to choose a place to preside over the overall plan. The Japanese Saionji and others all live permanently in the mountains and forests, but what is the difference in deciding on plans and resolving doubts? Moreover, at a time of emergency and survival, when the situation is critical, saving the country is not a matter of humility, and saving the country is not a time for concession. I know that the three elders are in the forest springs, but they have the party and the country in their hearts. The overall plan has been decided long ago, and there is no need to wait for the elders. However, what the people of the country have not yet finished hoping for is that in this extraordinary change, the whole country is in a state of crisis and shock, like suffering from a sudden illness. Emergency treatment can only treat the symptoms, and it cannot be saved by ordinary soup. Looking at the beginning of the European War, even in the advanced constitutional country of England, in the face of German aggression, it could not follow the old ways. Lei Zuo Zhi used the general superintendent of military supplies to form a national defense cabinet, which supported the crisis for several years. Today, China's crisis is a hundred times greater than England's. The enemy is at hand, and the daily reduction is hundreds of miles, but it is said that we can calmly sit and discuss, and bow our hands to govern. Can we or can we not? The people of the country already look to the government to deal with foreign affairs, and the government still does not comfort the people with foreign affairs, then it is not only contrary to the nature of the people, but also the world has never gained the trust of the people as it does today. If we lose this good opportunity for the whole country to unite, and do not mention the efforts of the whole country to deal with the national crisis, if the people of the country cannot seek it from the government, can they not save themselves together? Then what can the government say? I think that the officials in charge of our party and country should urgently respond to the people's hearts and quickly change the current government into a national defense organization. (A) Elect responsible persons with military and financial strength from all over the country, establish national defense government ministries and commissions, and strive to put their words into action and implement plans. And follow the example of the European War and set up several marshals of the navy, army, and air force, who are solely responsible for national defense. (B) Announce a general mobilization of all sectors of the country, suspend non-urgent government affairs, personnel, and consumer goods, and professions that are not suitable for war preparations, and order them to be changed to war preparation industries. (C) Implement national compulsory military service and compulsory labor service. One out of every two adults is conscripted to ensure that there are no surplus adults in the room and all are used for war preparations. (D) All factories, vehicles, and machines in the country shall be changed to direct and indirect war preparations. (E) All students of school age and professional personnel from all walks of life in the country shall be compiled into volunteer military service. (F) Follow the example of European and American citizens to bear war expenses, issue national defense bonds of 400 million yuan, and distribute and sell them in five years, so that each national will bear two yuan of war expenses per year. At the same time, establish a National Defense Fund Committee, which will be openly distributed and used by all sectors of the country to provide war preparations and to reorganize finances. (G) Each area with 1,000 people in the country shall set up a national shooting range, and the government shall supervise the implementation of live ammunition or reduced-medicine shooting, and stop all recreational sports. (H) During the national crisis, with a guarantee method, the people shall be allowed to freely possess self-defense guns. (I) During the national crisis, allow the Green Forest and the Communist Party to surrender and atone for their crimes. (J) During the national crisis, grant an amnesty once and forcibly conscript prisoners for military service and labor service, so that they can rehabilitate themselves. The above ten strategies are to revitalize the people's spirit and strengthen national power. If there is no other way, the government can truly determine the time limit and implement it in a unified manner on a specific date, and predetermine the implementation period on the day the national defense government is established, so as to relieve the people's difficulties. In this way, the day the national defense government is established will be the time when the people unanimously oppose foreign countries. Not only can it concentrate the strength of the whole country and unify the will of the whole country, but also the current chaotic political situation can avoid the futile efforts of neglecting cooperation. Even if the people of the country endure the pain for a moment, they will eventually reap the benefits in the long run. Even in diplomatic negotiations, it can truly receive the power of a solid backing. The rise and fall of the nation, the safety of the party and the country, depend on this move. The officials care about the national crisis and must have sympathy. Whether or not my humble opinion is appropriate, please guide and decide on it. I am an incompetent commoner who has been abandoned for a long time, and I should not raise my head and talk about national affairs. However, I have followed the Prime Minister for more than 20 years, witnessed the difficulty of creation, and participated in the development of the grass roots. How can I bear to sit idly by and watch the beautiful rivers and mountains be captured by our party? I feel that it is dangerous, so I dare not be silent. I shed tears and make a statement, hoping to be enlightened. Ye Xiasheng.

Recent News from the Youth Support Ma Group

▲ Organizing a Vanguard Team to Depart for the Front Line for a Bloody Battle

Since the Youth Support Ma Group left Shanghai last month for Yi, the situation along the way has been reported in various newspapers in this city. The group arrived in Beiping on the afternoon of the 3rd of this month by train from Pukou on the 30th of last month, passing through Xuzhou, Jinan, Tianjin and other places. Except for a few who could not endure hardship and those with "five-minute heat," most of them remained in Beiping and intensified military and political training, and organized a vanguard team to prepare to depart for the front line for a bloody battle. The rear advisory office of the group received a letter from the group yesterday, reporting on the recent situation of the group and the situation along the way to Beiping in detail. The details are as follows:

▲ Detention at Pukou Station: The group departed from Jinling University in Nanjing on the morning of the 28th of last month and arrived at Pukou Station. Due to the sudden drop in temperature and the flying snow in the air, many members of the group were thinly clothed. The leader of the group, Zhang Shaojie, instructed to temporarily park the train at the station and prepare coats on the other side of the river. The clothing problem was solved on the 30th, and then the special train departed, arriving in Xuzhou on the morning of the 31st.

▲ Welcome in Xuzhou: After the group arrived in Xuzhou, local people from all walks of life held a meeting at the Public Education Hall at 10:00 a.m. to welcome them. Many groups attended, totaling several thousand people. There were extremely passionate speeches. They left Xuzhou for the north at 2:00 p.m. on the first day. Representatives from all walks of life saw them off at the station and presented two flags.

▲ The Train Travels North: After leaving Xuzhou and heading north, the train did not stop at any stations along the way. On the morning of the 2nd, the train stopped in Jinan. The provincial government specially sent people to the station to welcome them, and the municipal government sent porridge and steamed buns to the station for the members to eat. At 1:10 p.m. on the 3rd, they arrived in Tianjin and stopped for two hours before changing trains to Beiping.

▲ Situation Upon Arrival in Beiping: They arrived in Beiping at about 4:00 p.m. on the 3rd. The train stopped at Fengtai, the station before Beiping. The Pacification Commissioner of Ping Sui specially sent an adjutant to inquire about everything. After arriving at the Qianmen Railway Station, the Commissioner's Office sent people to greet them and get off the train. The leader led the members into the city on foot and temporarily borrowed the Industrial University in Duan Wangfu Alley.

▲ General Situation of the Group: Since leaving Nanjing, the group has expelled one member for bad behavior and added five members. Mr. Bao Keming, who rushed from Suzhou to Beiping to register, has also joined. Now there are a total of 249 members of the group in Beiping. The office is now located in the Industrial University in Beiping. It plans to intensify military training in the shortest possible time and prepare everything for departure to the front.

Giant Book on the Northeast Problem Published

"The International Relations of Manchuria" is a masterpiece by C. Walter Young, a professor of political science at the University of Washington in the United States. He has conducted in-depth research on the Northeast issue. The book analyzes and comprehensively reviews the complex international relations of Manchuria over the years. The content is substantial and it can be considered a masterpiece on the Northeast issue. It has been translated into Chinese by Mr. Jiang Xingde and published by the Shenzhou Guoguang Society on Henan Road in this city. It was published in November of last year. The translation is faithful and fluent. The whole book has 200,000 words. A paperback book sells for 1.5 yuan. Major bookstores in this city and other cities are selling it.

Respectfully, in the "Local News" column of your newspaper on the 14th of this month, it was reported that the People's Organization Anti-Japanese National Salvation Joint Association held an inaugural meeting at the Youth Propaganda Corps, and our association was also listed as one of the participating organizations and elected as an executive committee member. Reader Communication

An Answer Regarding Domestic Goods Manufacturing: Heart Show

Our. Nation's. Yarn. Factory. Urgently. Needs. To. Self. Manufacture. Necessary. Items.

I am an employee of a domestic goods yarn factory (now foreign goods factories, usurping the role of the host, are filling the country, so I added the words "domestic goods" to distinguish them and express my grief). Although the equipment management in our factory cannot be said to be perfect, it is not so corrupt either. But I silently observe the present and consider the future, and I deeply feel that if we do not urgently seek improvement, not only will we not be able to develop, but I fear that even the previous prolonged existence will be impossible. Now, based on my limited perspective, I summarize that we should have a strict organization, complete facilities, and management that combines leniency and strictness. The machinery should be new and advanced, and the skills of the workers should be refined. The so-called

facilities should be scientific, the work should be standardized, and the technology should be mechanized. But the most important and fundamental method should be to quickly prepare to manufacture our own materials, such as lubricating oil and towing machine belts. Although these two items seem very small, we cannot manufacture them ourselves and rely on foreign goods. Once a war unfortunately occurs, or there is a boycott and the source is cut off, all machines will be forced to stop working, affecting the entire factory's operation. This matter, though small, can be used to understand larger issues. Another point that everyone should pay attention to is that we have been establishing modern textile industries for more than forty years, but the total number of spindles is only two million four hundred thousand. Therefore, Rong, the general manager of Wuxi Shenxin Yarn Factory, in order to expand the domestic textile industry, previously suggested to the government to borrow foreign spindles. After several consultations, the government has agreed to use the Boxer Indemnity of 1.3 million pounds as collateral to borrow 600,000 spindles from the United Kingdom. Adding one-quarter to the original number will increase production, which is certainly a fortunate event, but we still have to find a way to manufacture them ourselves, and not always rely on foreign spindles, so as not to be controlled by foreigners and plug the huge leakage. Our country's

yarn factory authorities should open their eyes to the future and make a permanent plan. If they seek only short-term gains and take advantage of the current opportunity to boycott Japanese goods, hoping to obtain huge profits, only considering the present and not the future, then I am afraid that once the wave of boycotts subsides, the yarn industry in our country, which is now flourishing, will suddenly show a miserable and depressed state again. Of course, the manufacture of domestic goods is not limited to the materials of yarn factories alone. I hope that for all the raw materials and items needed by various industries that are lacking in our country, everyone should study, pool their efforts and talents, and cooperate to manufacture them. Only in this way can we fundamentally promote domestic goods and boycott foreign goods. May our countrymen work hard and actively strive for this. (Bing)

Free Talk

An Indication of Japanese Internal Conflict with China

— Qingqu

Japan and our country are both located in East Asia. According to history, in the 28th year of Qin Shi Huang's reign, he toured the east, sealed Mount Tai, and performed the Feng and Shan sacrifices at Liangfu. He then toured the sea, seeking immortals. He also crossed the river south, touring the counties in the east, and summoned Confucian scholars from Lu. He returned to the foot of Mount Tai to discuss the Feng and Shan sacrifices. Afterwards, he toured the sea to the east, sacrificing to the eight gods of mountains and rivers. He ascended Langya to the south. Song Wuji and Xianmen Zigao from Yan claimed to have the Dao of Immortality, with the techniques of dissolving and transforming the body. Therefore, he sent people into the sea to seek Penglai, Fangzhang, and Yingzhou. It was said that these three divine mountains were in the Bohai Sea, where immortals and the elixir of immortality were. Thereupon, a Fangshi, Xu Fu (or Xu Shi), submitted a memorial, requesting to be allowed to fast and with three thousand young men and women to seek them. As soon as he entered the sea, the ships encountered the sea, and they all used the wind as an explanation, saying, "We have not been able to reach them, but we have seen them." However, there is no record of his return. Therefore, those who have studied this historical site have repeatedly doubted and could not believe it. However, the ancestor of the three islands must undoubtedly belong to Xu.

However, there are no records in Japanese historical books. It is said that because of racial relations, it was feared that it would be detrimental to the future progress of the country, so it was deleted. Only a type of burial code remains in the secret cabinet. Three years ago, I heard from a gentleman who had traveled to the East that Xu Fu's tomb is indeed located near Shingu Town near Kishu Kumanoura in Japan. Its area is extremely vast. The tombstone stands tall, and ancient cypresses reach the sky, with a circumference that can be encompassed. There are seven tombs of those who were buried with him nearby, all with inscriptions that can be examined. They are scattered in the "Continued Topography of Kii". I regret not having seen it. Therefore, the details of Xu's eastward crossing have not been collected. To verify its belief. Yesterday, from Qin Jun Jiliao, I obtained a book "Records of Countries East of the Sea", which contains, "The first emperor liked the immortal method, and ordered Xu Fu to lead three thousand young men and women, carrying grain seeds and hundreds of tools, to go to Penglai to seek it. Not finding it, he feared punishment. He dared not return. At that time, it was the 72nd year of Emperor Kōrei in Japan. He then entered the Japanese nationality.” Therefore, Xu's departure and no return can be verified in this book.

I still remember that in the 26th and 27th years of the Qing Guangxu period, the envoy to Japan, Li Shuchang, crossed the sea to visit his tomb and wrote a record of it. Unfortunately, his text cannot be found now. Otherwise, it will definitely be possible to find its origin. The first record of the islanders wearing grass garments can be found in "Tribute of Yu". Since the Han Dynasty, there have been no reports of Japanese pirates. This is because they want to love fresh flowers, and the land is rich and fertile. The five states and seven roads, and the five hundred and seventy-three counties of the three islands, are all happy lands. Surrounded by the sea, the rulers and ministers protect themselves and do not admire China. Those who study human races also believe that because their land belongs to Asia and their skin color is also yellow, and their surnames, lifestyles, and customs are no different from those in China, except for the Ezo of Hokkaido, who are completely different. This can be compared with Ji Zi being enfeoffed in Korea and Zheng Chenggong's refuge in Taiwan.

It is not unfounded. It is said that today people with the surname Qin are mostly descendants of Fu and are extremely prosperous. Since the Meiji Restoration, they began to change to other surnames. There is a Fujisawa Station Fukuoka Heiichirō, who is a descendant of Fu. And the famous doctor Xu of Wakayama Prefecture is a direct descendant of Kangzong. Although there are no genealogies to prove it, the bloodline of Xu must be abundant. Today, the wooden clogs forget where they came from, and are competing with China. If the lips are gone, the teeth will be cold. Only considering aggression as a good strategy, alas. I recite the sentence "We are originally from the same root, why are we so eager to harm each other?", and I am not only sad for myself, but also regret it for them.

Feng Huanzhang and Jiang Jieshi

— Zizai

Feng Yuxiang and Jiang Zhongzheng were originally sworn brothers. How their two people’s views and policies about governing the party and state, will be discussed later. Now, I will only describe one or two anecdotes for after-dinner conversation.

When Jiang and Feng met for the second time in Zhengzhou, Ma Fuxiang was Feng's confidant at the time. Seeing that the two were determined to cooperate, he persuaded them to exchange pledge cards and become brothers. Jiang and Feng agreed. So, they exchanged sworn brotherhood agreements with the ancestral three generations records, and became brothers of different surnames. Later, Mr. Ma often said to people, "I was the matchmaker for Jiang and Feng's sworn brotherhood." He was happy and joyful.

Although Jiang and Feng became brothers, Feng's salutation to Jiang's telegrams was always with "respectful start”. The salutation at the top always called him "Commander-in-Chief Revered Examination", and the title was "Your Excellency". The closing signature was "Your subordinate Feng Yuxiang". Jiang immediately sent a letter of humble refusal, saying that their friendship was like siblings, and they should not address each other in this way. In the future, please continue to call each other as brothers, which is more intimate. Feng then stated that public affairs are public, and private matters cannot be abolished. Although private friendship is as brothers, in terms of official duties, he is a superior and I an subordinate, and I must do so. If so, then both agreed that except for public affairs, the words "Your Excellency" etc. should still be used, and for everything else they would call each other "Brother Jieshi" and "Little Brother Xiang" etc. to show the distinction and to maintain both public and private matters.

When Jiang went north to Lanfeng to meet Feng, and Feng invited Jiang to review the troops, the troops stationed in Lanfeng happened to be those of Shi Yousan. The Northwest Army was famous for its well-disciplined forces, especially the Shi Army. The soldiers' swordsmanship was superb, making the viewers dazzled and astonished. Then he ordered the officers to demonstrate the pole climbing technique. Shi Yousan showed off his skills on the spot, took off his military uniform, and went bare-chested on the pole. He thoroughly demonstrated his unique skills. Jiang praised him in admiration. Shi joined Feng's army at the age of sixteen. He was intelligent and agile. From the time he was a soldier to the time he became a junior officer, he always topped his class in the tactical exams. The pole climbing technique was his unique skill, and he could be called the best in the entire army.

The Tomb of Li Fengjie

— Yi Zang

When I went to Zhangjiakou in the past, I walked from Nankou across the Juyong Pass, climbed the Badaling, and arrived at Qinglongqiao, taking a tour of the Great Wall. One day, I and my friend Yan Wenjin went to the tomb of Li Fengjie. Enduring dangers and climbing steep slopes, we finally reached the place. The tomb is located on the ridge of Badaling, north of the Juyong Pass, backed by mountains and facing the valley. The white soil is bright and clean. There are several dilapidated houses nearby, all moved in by people from Huailai, who are engaged in sheep herding. According to the local people, there used to be thirty or forty households, half Manchu and half Han. Later, due to the continuous cycle of soldiers and bandits, many moved south to Changping. However, the ruins and broken tiles still remain. The most peculiar thing is that among the dark blue mountains and black peaks, which are interlaced for hundreds of miles, and the steep cliffs that stand thousands of feet high, how could there be a pile of white soil to bury a fragrant soul? Today, the remaining steles and broken pillars are indistinguishable. However, the local people have passed down the story that the tomb was originally yellow soil, but it suddenly turned into white fat after being struck by lightning. Later generations dismissed this as a lie and said that Fengjie returned to the capital with the emperor in the same carriage at that time. However, the official history does not record it because it involves reversal and appropriation. Therefore, later generations have no way to judge its authenticity. Only in the anecdotes of the wild scholars is there a description of the romantic affair of Emperor Zhengde of the Ming Dynasty playing with dragons and phoenixes, which proves that Fengjie died suddenly on the way. The tomb on Badaling is undoubtedly Fengjie's. When Chen Hao rebelled, the Emperor went on a personal expedition. On the way to Xuanhua, the Emperor went out in disguise and suddenly saw a woman in a tavern. She was about fifteen or sixteen years old, with a graceful appearance. The Emperor carefully examined her and became increasingly infatuated. The Emperor saw that there was no one in the tavern and entered the tavern to buy wine. At that time, Fengjie's father was out, so Fengjie was tending the stove. Because Fengjie brought wine to the seat, the Emperor mistakenly thought that she was a prostitute. His soul was shaken, and he suddenly embraced her. Fengjie screamed. The Emperor covered her mouth and said, "I am the Emperor. If you follow me, wealth and honor can be achieved immediately." Before that, Fengjie had a dream that she had turned into a bright pearl and was being played with by a blue dragon. Suddenly, she turned into smoke and clouds and dissipated. Hearing the Emperor's words, she suddenly realized and allowed the Emperor to close the door. Her silk dress was loosened, and she was still a virgin. The Emperor was overjoyed. At that time, Fengjie's father heard the shouts and rushed to rescue her. The door was tightly locked. He quickly called for help from the guard, who swarmed in. They suspected that it was a thief. When the door opened, the Emperor stood with his sword, and the soldiers prostrated themselves. The Emperor scolded them and ordered them to send Fengjie back to the Leopard Room, ennobled her father as a third-rank minister, and bestowed a thousand taels of gold. He wanted to ennoble Fengjie as a concubine and ordered her to choose for herself. Fengjie firmly declined. The Emperor saw that her black dress made her even more charming, so he did not force her to change her palace clothes. Later, the Emperor wanted to return to the capital with Fengjie in the same carriage. When they arrived at Juyong Pass, the wind and thunder roared. Feng also saw the four large stone statues carved at the entrance of the Pass, their faces lifelike. She became dizzy and fell off her horse. The Emperor personally helped her up and retreated quickly. He stationed at the traveling palace. Fengjie knew that her fortune was thin and that she could not pass the palace ban. She persuaded the Emperor to return quickly. The Emperor could not bear to abandon her. Fengjie cried bitterly and died. The Emperor ordered her to be buried on the mountain of the Pass, with special honors. The yellow soil tomb was used, and it turned into white fat overnight. It can be said that the spirit did not dare to accept it. Although this is the saying of the "Yan Shu", those who personally visited Fengjie's tomb on Badaling today all believe that the Shandong Li Bai lamented that his origin was correct. Moreover, the official history also records that the Emperor was in the Leopard Room and that the officials presented memorials to persuade him, but he did not accept them. He suddenly died on the way. As for the fact that the father mistook the brother at Liyuan, it cannot be verified.

Random Notes on Japanese Swords

— Zheng Yimei

The Japanese respect martial arts and like to kill. They often wear Japanese swords as ornaments. There are two types, large and small. The large ones are called "Tachi," and the small ones are called "Wakizashi." During the Zhao Song Dynasty, the Japanese once paid tribute with them. Ouyang Yongshu had a "Song of the Japanese Sword," which was widely recited. According to Japanese historical records, the art of making swords began in the Heian period (during the Tang Dynasty in China). By the Chengging era (during the Five Dynasties period), its production began to be refined. During the reign of Emperor Uda (during the Yuan Dynasty in China), two craftsmen, Yoshimitsu and Masamune, were especially famous. They were no less than Gan Jiang and Mo Xie, who made swords in our country. Now, these swords are rare. The imperial family often uses them as gifts. I still remember that the Japanese Emperor gave Chiang Kai-shek a Japanese sword a few years ago. I don't know if this sword still exists. I sincerely hope that he will swear an oath and go straight to the barbarian island. Then, with this sword, he will quickly annihilate the barbarians.

Therefore, the literary scholar Bi Jian'an's Guangxu Palace Poem, one of several poems, says: "The Qiong flute and silver pipes sing the golden elixir, the wonderful dance and clear song move the holy face. Alas, the Japanese sword leaves a matter of regret, the cherry blossoms are withered and fallen to the human world.” The postscript says that Zhang Jian's "Tsui Yu Tang Poetry Talks" says: Emperor Dezong greatly appreciated the actor Yu Zhuang'er and performed a new play "Ten Golden Elixirs" in the palace. Before he could remove his makeup, Emperor Dezong summoned him to the palace and took his hand and looked back and said, "This son can be called both talented and virtuous." The Empress, because he was near the throne, was about to complain to the Empress Dowager Cixi. The Emperor was afraid and used the Japanese sword that Yu was wearing as a real weapon. He was about to be charged with the crime of carrying a weapon in front of the Emperor. He waved him out and said, "Send him to the Ministry of Justice." Yu then reported his illness and was never summoned again. There is a poem about this matter: "Zheng Yingtao danced and sang in front of the palace, the ten golden elixirs were unusually high-pitched. After all, the sage was holding the big picture, and the Japanese sword was taken off under the carved balustrade." This palace story involves Japanese swords, making it even more charming.

The Japanese Bushido actually began with Minamoto Yoritomo. Fearing that the last members of the Taira clan would fall into Judo and be weak, he advocated martial arts and practiced various martial arts. He became famous and well known. Until today, the imperial family still has Bushido to defend themselves. They hold a competition once a year. The winner will be rewarded with gold. They can become rich. The Bushido mostly excel in internal skills. If you wrestle with them, you cannot restrain their arms. Otherwise, after the luck has gone, the hands cannot be removed, or the nails will come off and the fingers will be reversed, and the extreme pain will make you fall down. Using Japanese swords is the ultimate skill of Bushido. When a certain celebrity traveled to Japan, his bamboo branch words had the line "Relying on Japanese swords to awaken the national soul," which is a factual record.

Record of Things Seen and Heard in the Old Capital

— Zhu An

Strange Clock

"Notes on the West Qinghua" says, "The Great Bell of Jiaotai Hall in the palace is considered the standard. The hall has three rooms. The east room is equipped with a clepsydra, almost full. It uses about a bucket of water a day. Since the Qianlong era, it has long been abandoned. The west room is where the Great Bell is located. It is as tall as the room. Climbing up the ladder, the key is turned and the spring is wound up. It is only opened again a month later. There has been no difference for decades. The sound travels far, reaching outside the Qianqing Gate. It is still the old system from the Wanli period." It also says, "There is a clock in the Neifu. The lower frame has a copper man. He is about four or five inches long. He is kneeling with one foot bent. In front of him is a sand tray. When the clock rings, the copper man holds a tube in one hand and draws sand in the tray to make the four characters 'Tian Xia Tai Ping' (world peace). When the sound of the clock disappears, the writing is also finished. It is said that it was also made when the Italian priest came to China for the first time.”

In the past, when I read this record, I always thought it was absurd. Now that the Forbidden City is open, the treasures of the inner government's celestial sphere are all revealed. I realized that Shen Shi was actually speaking based on what he saw. Jiaotai Hall was originally the place where the imperial seals were stored. It was rarely visited on weekdays. Therefore, there was enough space in the hall to store the Great Bell. Among the clocks in the country, the largest and most ancient one is probably unparalleled. The old clocks and watches stored in the Wuying Hall of the Ancient Cultural Relics Exhibition are even more numerous. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, old craftsmen were hired to repair the machines one by one for display. They were all worth seeing. One of them had a box door that opened automatically every time the clock rang. Crystal sand flowed, making a rustling sound, like a waterfall. Then, birds sang on the branches, their songs were melodious and pleasing to the ear. They fluttered their wings and flew to other branches, and then they lingered for a long time before stopping. Its workmanship is hardly human. There are also similar legends from the past. It is said that a certain governor of Guangdong during the Jiaqing and Daoguang periods sought a craftsman to make a machine that would write the four characters "Wan Shou Wu Jiang" (long live the emperor). He planned to present it to the palace. Because he was stingy with his expenses, he was questioned by the eunuch. He said that if the machine suddenly broke when writing the word "Wu," the disaster would be unpredictable. The governor was afraid and stopped. At that time, the craftsmen's attention was so focused on playthings. It is no wonder that the elders strongly criticized the strange and ingenious skills of Westerners.

In the year of Jia Shen in the Qianlong period, a certain country in the West presented eighteen copper puppets who could perform an entire play of the West Chamber. The puppets were about a foot tall. Their bodies, ears, eyes, hands, and feet were all cast in copper. Their hearts and intestines were all connected by keys. Like an automatic clock, each scene had a fixed process of inserting the key and opening the lock. If it was opened incorrectly, they would sit, lie down, walk, and speak incorrectly. Zhang Ying, Hong Niang, Hui Ming, Fa Cong, and others could put on clothes from the box. Their body movements, gestures, salutes, advances, and retreats were all lifelike. They just couldn't sing. After a scene was over, they would take off their clothes and lie in the box. When it was their turn, they would stand up again. In the middle of the scene, they would stand up on the carpet. This is what a certain notebook recorded. There is no such thing in the Forbidden City today. The clocks and watches in the Forbidden City are mostly products from 17th-century England. They have the manufacturer's mark. They are not only known for their gorgeous decorations and harmonious sounds. Their precision has lasted for a long time without any error. There is nothing like this today. In addition, the collections of old families and noble clans are also quite numerous. Many of the smaller ones have fallen into the hands of merchants. The heavier ones that cannot be obtained are still there. I think that those who have a fondness for this can compile a "Chronicle of Clocks in the Old Capital," which will surely be widely circulated. The people of the capital also call watches "clocks," which is also a tradition from ancient times.

The Story of Ma Shuanglou (12)

— Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

Episode 2: Mocking Good Teachers, Spreading Bad News, Home Encountering Robbery, Pitying Intimate Friends, Comforting Sad Feelings, Spring Awakening in the Inn

Wei Zhuomou ran into a wall. He paused slightly, but then regained his composure. Like an actor reciting lines in a play, he asked in a strange voice, "Hey, I see you have something very heavy on your mind today. Since I have nothing to do, let me guess." Then he scratched his head and cheeks and did another set of delicate acting. Only then did he say, "Oh, oh, oh, I guessed it. Let me ask you first, has An Yutian come these past two days? You're probably missing him, right?" Liang Xiaoyun turned her face away and said, "You're guessing wildly again. Why would I miss him for no reason? It's just that he hasn't come these past few days. Let's talk about serious matters. Have you seen him? Do you know why he hasn't been out for several days?" Wei Zhuomou smiled and said, "How can you be sure that he hasn't been out for several days? Just because he hasn't come to you, does that mean he can't go anywhere else?" This counter-question left her speechless and a little ashamed, causing a slight flush to rise on her powdery cheeks. She became even more coquettish and said, "I don't care about you. You're too hateful. I was just asking you about him seriously. Why are you always going against me? I'm not talking to you anymore. Please leave." Wei Zhuomou smiled and said, "I can't leave. I know the most details about his affairs. I came here today because even if you didn't ask me, I was originally going to tell you about it after class. Now that you've angered me, I can't just tell you the details casually. Let me just reveal a little bit. He's gotten into big trouble. This trouble is very big. It's not only terrible, but also unbearable. If you want to know what happens next, listen to the next episode. Since you're not happy talking to me, I don't need to say any more. Excuse me, I'll ask for leave. I'm leaving. You don't need to make a fuss." After saying that, he picked up a book and really stood up, pretending to take a step to leave. She hurriedly grabbed his hand and stamped her feet and said, "Okay, you playful Mr. Don't pretend anymore. Hurry up and tell me. What big trouble did he get into? Is it serious? Tell me quickly." Wei Zhuomou said he was leaving, but he was just playing around. Naturally, he stabilized his body and said slowly, "Seeing how anxious you are, it's obvious that you really care about him. If I tell you the truth about his unfortunate disaster, I'm a little afraid that you won't be able to bear it. But you're asking me so hard, how can I not tell you? There's no other way. Please calm your mind and be brave enough to listen." Liang Xiaoyun suddenly interjected, "You're saying it's so scary. I remember he said he had a headache when he came here last time. Could it be that he's really fallen ill?" Wei Zhuomou hurriedly waved his hand and said, "No, that's not it. Don't interrupt. He's very strong. He can't be knocked down by your illness. Why are you being so anxious? This time his disaster is more serious than anything else. I'm from the same hometown as him. I know all about his family's affairs. He has elderly parents in the hall, and also a weak younger brother. He alone … Yu family is in the hometown…
